Odaanaang bimibatoowan odayan gaa-bimaagonebizod. Mishawagaam waasaashkaa. Gichi-onzaamaanimad. Waasaashkaa iwe zaaga'igan. Gii-nameshin a'aw ginebig o'omaa gii-pimi-ayaagwen. Oshkiinamoog gaa-gii-pimi-miikanaakewaad. Ganabaj zhebaa gii-pimi-ayaawag. Niwii-pabaamaakwii noopimiing. Niwii'-andawagoodoo. Wenda-gabe-ishkwaa-naawakwe babaam... obabaama'anaan iniwen waawaashkeshiwan a'awe gaawased. Owii-ikoshimaan iniw mitigoon gaa-aazhawishininid imaa miikanaang. Gii-aazhawibizo imaa eshpaanig aazhogan. Gidanoonigoo ji-o-wiindaman i'iw oshki-aazhogan. Ogotaan ji-aazhawishkang iwe gete-aazhoganish. Dabasaakosin aazhogan Gichi-mookomaanakiing gaa-izhi-aazhawamog. Zhaaganaashiiwakiing onji-maadamon. Mii go imaa godagiing gaa-pabaamanokiid 'aw gwiiwizens. Gii-sagaakwa'igaazo awe gizhe-manidoo imaa aazhideyaatigong. Gaawiin gegoo gii-inamanjigesii aana-gii-izhinizha'ond iwidi Waashtanong. Mii iwidi gaa-izhinizha'amaan Waashtanong gaa-kiizhig.. gaa-kiizhibii'igaadeg 'i onaakonigewin. Gii-pabiiwishkam awe waawaashkeshi gaa-... gaa-pima'anag. Indaga dawinamaw 'iw desa'on aw niningwan. Mii imaa ge-izhi-bagidoomaad iniw waawaashkeshiwan. Odazhiikawaan iniw waawaashkeshiwan gaa-paashkizwaad. Nina'aangish gii-paashkizwaad ini waawaashkeshiwan, agaawaa ogii-kashkinanaan. Onandawaabamaan iniw gaa-maakinawaad waawaashkeshiwan. Gaawiin geyaabi ogashki'aasiin ji-bimibizo'aad odaabaanan; onzaam gaawiin zaabaabisii. Babiiskijiitaa babaa-ayaad. Gego bimibatwaadangen gibaashkizigan. Anaamisag dazhewag waawaabiganoojiinyag. Waawaabiganoojiinyan naa oniimamaan a'a gaazhagenzhish Wiisakwemagad odaabaan bimibideg miikanaang. Diba'iganaatig omaa bimaakosidoon. Aaniish ge omaa ba-onji-nanaamadabid wa'awe. | Aana go naa mawadishiwe. Aabiji-waasamoog igiweg manidoog ba-ayaawaad. Indigo naage gii-waasikwiingwe wa'awe. Giminikwe ina. Gaawiin abisii. Megwaa babaamaadizi. Gii-paakaakosin i'iw waasechigan gabe-dibik. Gii-piindigese a'aw obikwaanaajiinh. Mashkawaabikad iw waasechigan. Baakibidoon waasechigan. Ani-gashkiidibikak gidaa-gibiiga'aanaan giwaasechiganan. Ingii-piidoon ingo-minikwaajigan iwe waasamoo-bimide. Babaamaadagaa 'a nigig. Waasizowag igiw manidoominensag. Gizhii-waasizo awe asin waabishkizid. Mii go ingoji niiyo-diba'iganeg ashi-aabita bi-waaseyaag. Weweni bimibatoon. Giga-bakiteshin. Odaanaang bimibatoowan odayan gaa-bimaagonebizod. Zhebaa ingii-pi-aazhoge'adoo. Ishkwaa-naawakweg niwii'-ani-aazhoge'adoo. Gii-aazhawishkaawaad imaa ziibiinsing gii-pimaadagaaziiwag. Ona'itawaan oosan ezhi-gikinoo'amaagod. Nindabiitawaa wa'awe memaanjigozid bebmaadizid. Minwaakwad iwe baaga'adowaanaatig. Giishpin gashkiiwakwak gii-niibing, zagimekaa. Ogii'-onzaami-zhiiwitaagana'aan onaboobiikaan. Aanawendaagozi ji-giizhitoopan waakaa'igan; onzaam gitimishki. Madwesidoon zhinawa'oojigan. Mii 'iw zhaangaso-diba'iganeg ji-madwesidood 'iw godotaagan. Giishpin madwesidood nimbiiwaabikoonsim, ninga-gagwejimaa ji-anokiitawag. Bi-anokiin. "Ondaashaan omaa bi-izhaan," nindig nookomis. Agamiing iwidi bi-ondose. Aaniin ezhi-wiindemagak iwe oodena gaa-bi-gibikamang, Bi-makadewaanakwagoode 'iwe aanakwad iwidi ningaabii'anong. Gaawiin ganage gii-pi-izhaasiin. Miskwaabikizi aw giizis ba-zaagajiwed. Aabanaabam a'awe ba-debinaagozid, aaniin ezhi'od. Zhebaa ingii-pi-aazhoge'adoo. Ishkwaa-naawakweg niwii'-ani-aazhoge'adoo. Mii 'iw gii-tazhwegiwebiniged 'awe gaa-pi-mawine'ond. Wii-makizinataadiwag. Ingii-kabenaagoomin makizinataading. Aaniin enataadiwaad? / Ganabaj makizinataadiwag. Gii-kwekitaa aana-gii-anami'aad a'awe nimishoone. Naaweg bagiwaanegamig onji-onjigaa . Aandi gaa'-izhi-dazhwegisidooyan bagiwaanegamig ji-baateg. / Ogiji-bikwasin ingii'-izhi-dazhwegisidoon. Bangii ogii-minikwen 'iw doodooshaaboo. Daga ningodonaagaans naazikamawishin nitii ge-minikweyaan. Nindaanis ogii-minikwen doodooshaaboo. Ningii-minikwen waashkobaagamig. Wiinaagamin nibi zaaga'iganiing. Gego minikweken. Mishawagaam iwidi debinaagwad 'iw jiimaanens bemibideg. Agaawaa bapagidanaamo awe gaa-agwaayaadagaad. Mishawagaam gii-ondaadagaa. Mishawagaam waasaashkaa. Mishawagaam ondoonda'oonaan iniw ogaawan. Ingii-tebaabamaa biida'adood gaa-mazina'amawid zhooniyaan gaa'-izhi-gaajibani'od. Ogii-siiga'aan iwe zhiiwaagamizigan imaa biskitenaaganing. Mii imaa gii-abid 'a goon. Mii imaa gii-pigiwiziged nimaamaayiban, Anzig nitaa-noojigiigoowensiwe. Giiwitaabiwag gikinoo'amawaaganag. Dibaajimowag ezhi-anishinaabewinikaazowaad miinawaa ezhi-odoodemiwaad. Zhebaa ogii'-wiinaan ge-izhi-anishinaabewinikaazonid. Miiwan iniwe wiiyawen'enyan. Manidoo-giizisoons gii-oshkagoojin awasi-dibikong. Awasi-dibikong gii'-madwe-zaaga'am aakoziiwigamigong. Giinitamawind ina giga-o-bawa'aamin manoomin. Giinitamawind gidigoomin ji-gaagiigidoyang. Ningii-pashkonawaa; onzaam gizhiikaabatoo gii-aazhawa'adoobatood. Naawaakigan ogii-sagamigoon ezigaan. Gaawiin ingodinoo wiidookaazoyan. Megwaa bimosed a'aw inini gaa-izhi-gawised. Ondaasikana bimose awe akiwenzii. Waaboozwayaan gidaa-gibishe'onan giishpin aazhawagaakowin zaaga'igan gii-gichi-gisinaag. Napaajaya'ii inagakeyaa ingii-pimibizomin imaa miikanaang. Ningaabii'anong inagakeyaa ogii-ina'anaan oosan. Iwidi inagakeyaa izhiwizh. O'owe inagakeyaa gidaa-inagoodoon ni-waabanjigaadegiban. Aaniin inagakeyaa enawendiwaad. Gigii-tebashkina'aag ina zhiishiibag imaa gimashkawaakwajijigani-makakong. Wa, gichi-mashkawaagamin i'iw ishkodewaaboo gaa-mina'igooyaan. Ingii-nagishkawaa indawemaa iwidi zhigaag... zhigaagong gii-shiimaaganishiiwiyaan. Mamadwetoo iwidi awasisag. Namanj ezhichigegwen. Awegwen igo gaa-mamadwetood agwajiing dibikong. Ingii-kashkaabika'aan indoodaabaan degoshinaan imaa endaayaan. Owi-gashkaabika'an iwe bizhikiiwigamig. Gigii-gashkaabika'aan ina iwe odaabaan. Gashkaabika'an gidoodaabaan ingoji wii'-nibaayan gichi-oodenaang. Gashkaabika'an gimiikana gaa-bi-onji-zaagijibizoyan. Ogii-chekibiinaan obakwezhigaansiman ji-nookaabaawenid. Daga izhiwizhishin aakoziiwigamigong. Niwii-wi-waabamaa mashkikiiwinini. Nindaakoz. Gii-kwiinawi-inendam gii-pi-wiindamawind gichi-aakozinid ookomisan. Aakoziyaan naa gaa-izhi-wiisagaapineyaan. Nisayenh ganabaj bagidenimo. Gaawiin ogashkitoosiin geyaabi ji-wiisinid; onzaam gichi-aakozi. Jiigi-gizhaabikizigan onji-baasan gidazhiganan. Mii iwidi gaa-pimi-inamog ozide-miikana jiigi-ziibi. Mii imaa bemi-izhising oodena jiigi-zaaga'igan. Jiigi-aasamisag ate nibewin. Gego izhaaken imaa jiigi-gizhaabikiziganing. Onzaamaabikide onzaam. Nametoo imaa odaabaaniiwigamigong gii-andawaabanjigegwen. Onandomaandaan gaa-jaagidewimaatenig. Geyaabi babaamisewag aandegwag. Gaawiin mashi ando-biboonishisiiwag. Odaana-gii-wewebiniketawaan aana-wii-noogibinaad iniwen gaa-bimibizonid. Ogii-noogibinaan ini odayan jibwaa-niminaakowaad. Aaniish enamog 'iw miikana. Maanamonoon iniw miikanan. Aabiding iidog gii-pabimose 'aw mindimooyenh imaa miikanaang. Miikanaang izhi-wanii'amaw amik. Ogii-pabaa-gikinawaaji'aawaan iniwen mitigoon ge-giishkizhomind. Indaga o-binibidoon ini apishimoniiginan. Ingii-nanawiz aana-... aana-gii-kiiwaseyaan. Ingii-waniikenan indanwiiman. Ningii'-nanawiz gii-naadagweyan. Gaawiin awiya ningii'-nagwaanaasii. Gaawiin gegoo ningii'-nagwaadanziin. Ogii-naajinizha'aan omaa wenji-biitood awe... awegodowen dinowa. Ingii-waambandaan iwidi gichi-jiimaan gechi-mangadeyaag. Ozhitamawishin ge-nawapoyaan. Mashkodeng ingii-pabaa-inaab ziigwanong. Gii-aapidendi awe gaa-kiiwooded ziigwanong. Obi-zaagidoomaan ogwizisensan. Dikinaaganing dakobizowan. Gaawiin minwamanji'osii gaa-onji-nanaandomod. Zhooniyaa nindayaawaa nizhooniyaa-mashkimodaang. Ogii-andoojiishkaan 'iw ozhooniyaa-mashkimodens gaa-paninang imaa gashkii-dibikatenig ji-... odaabaaniiwigamigong. Niminwamanji' igo. Gaawiin igo niminomanji'osii. Gaawiin minwamanji'osii gaa-onji-nanaandomod. Naanginigoziwag igiweg opiniig imaa baanzowaad mashkimodaang. Aanawi go ogii-gikendaan ji-wekwaaseying iwe ziinzibaakwad. Gaawiin aapiji ogikendanziin omiikana gaa-onji-wanibizod. Gego memwech wiindamawaaken. Aazha ogikendaan waa'-izhichiged. Gaawiin ingii-gikendanziin waa-izhichigeyaan, gaa-izhi-gagwejitooyaan. Ogikendaanaawaa gakina gegoo. Bekaa bimibizon aazhawibizowin zaaga'igan gaa-gikendanziwan. Maagizhaa gidaa-bitaabikishin Gego izhinoo'waaken giiji-bimaadizii aanawi go gii-bizhishigwaabikak. Ogiji-nibewin daningwaamo bizhiins. Nimookamanji'. Ganabaj niwii'-agigokaa. Apane ninjaachaam. Giiyaabi na ishpi-giizhigadinig gii-oninamaad. Bangii aanakwadowan. Oshkinaweg bakitejii'igewag iwidi jiigikana. Aapiji go inzinigwenimaa awe indooshkinawem. Mii 'i gii-maajidaabii'iwed. Nisawi-waakaa'igan ningii'-waabamaag oshkinaweg dazhi-zagaswaawaad. Gii-panoomigo gaa-onji-bookogaadeshing awe oshkinawe. Giiwitaabiwag gikinoo'amawaaganag. Dibaajimowag ezhi-anishinaabewinikaazowaad miinawaa ezhi-odoodemiwaad. Wawaasaabizowag igiweg bizhikiwag mekwaasenodawagwaa Niin iko ningii-mimigosaga'ige gii-wiinisagaamagak 'i endaayaang. Wiinisagaani endaad nookoo. Niwii'-awi-giziisaginamawaa. Gaawiin ingii-gikendanziin waa-izhichigeyaan, gaa-izhi-gagwejitooyaan. Babiiwizhenyiwa' oniijaanisa'. Gego zaaminaaken awe manidoosh. Zhebaa ningii-noondawaa a'aw animosh madwe-migid. Gaawiin ninoondaagosiin a'aw inini. Ganabaj gagiibishe. Awasisag iwidi namadabi awe endwewemad. Ningikenimaa iwidi ayaad. Ninoondawaa megaded. Awiya ningii'-noondawaa biibaagid gii-biidaabang. Ningii'-noondawaa "gaawiin" ikidod. Gaawiin ganabaj odaa-gashkitoon. Gagwe-noondaw gwayak ekidod. Ningii'-noondaagoo na gaa-gii'-ikidowaan. Ogii-nibiikaadaan i'iwe noomazhaan wenji-jiikaakiziged. Indaga mikamaw odooshkiinzhigokaanan awe gimishoomis. Anzhikewabi awe gimishoomisinaan. Gego babaamenimaaken gimishoomis. Megwaa apaakozige. Aweniban naa gii-animosed a'awe, ganabaj gii-ni-bake. Ogii-bakewinaan iniw odikweman. Giishpin okawi'ad awiya wawaaga'amiid, gaag a'a gaa-bimikawed. Gii'-agozigwaji gii-dasoozod amik. Gaawiin ngii-tebinaasii awe asabaabiins ishpaya'ii iwidi gaa-achigaazod. Nookomis gii'-achigaazo gikaawigamigong; onzaam obwaanawitoon ji-bami'idizod. Ningoshko'ig a'aw gaa-saagewed nimishoomis. Aaboodazhigane. Ganabaj wewiib gii-piitazhigane. Anaamakamig aanind daawag awesiinyensag. Anaamakamig dazhigiwag bagaanag. Anaamakamig bimaabikisin i'iw nibi. Anaamakamig maa ingii-kaanaa nzhooniyaam. Anaamakamig gii-onji-mookii a'aw obiigomagakii Nising naa ninjiibaakwe noongom. Nising ningii-paashkizwaa mooz gaa-gii-piinag zhebaa. Wenipanizi baanizhaawind awe ogaa. Wenipanizi debibinind awe mishtadim. Bebooninig gii-nitaawigi. Aapiji goonikaa noongom biboong. Dagwaagong ningii-manisemin wii-aabajitooyaang biboong. Aaniin epiichi-biboong. Bakaan gewiin odizhisidoon iwe nagamon ena'amaang. Mii 'i gaa-inanoonind ji-odaabii'iwed gaa-onji-babaamidaabii'iwed. Madweyaabideshin a'aw gwiiwizens epiitajid. Indaga bi-ashidaakonan 'i diba'iganaatig. Niwii-anda-gikendaan aaniin epiitaag. Ningaabii'anong inagakeyaa izhinoo'ige ondaanimak. Gakaabikaaning gii-onjibide iwe gaa-pooniimagak bemiseg. Wiinjiigimaagwad zaaga'amoowigamig. Gabe-onaagosh owaazakonendamowaan iniwen nenaa'idaabaanikenid. Gii-minochige gii-asanjigod ini ozhooniyaaman imaa zhooniyaawigamigong. Zhebaa omaa gii-pi-boonii migizi ogidabak. Gego omaa atooken ogidabak. Gidoonaaganens da-diitibiwebaasin. Ogii-andoojiishkaan 'iw ozhooniyaa-mashkimodens gaa-paninang imaa gashkii-dibikatenig ji-... odaabaaniiwigamigong. Gii-aatawesewan ini waasigani-waaz... waazakonenjiganan wenji-gashkii-dibikateg. Ningii'-agozideshkawaa wanakozid. Nimiijinan ziinzibaakwadoonsan. Oningwanendaan i'iw ziinzibaakwadoons. Aaniin ekoniked. O-wewiibim. Ogii-minozaan iwe gichikonayeziganaaboo zhiiwitaagani-gookooshan imaa gii-apaabowed. Adaawewigamigong apatoo. Neniswi ningii-apatoomin zaaga'iganiing. Aandi epatood. O'owapii onaabani-giizis angizod, anooj apatoowag waaboozoog. Indaga o-wewebaabiigin 'a abinoojiinyens debwewidang. Ningii-tangishkawaa animozhish gaa-bi-gagwe-dakwamid. Niizho-mininj gii'-maajiigi noongom gaa-biboong noozhis Dana. Awe mazinikojigan wezhi'ad, weweni izhi'. Dibishkoo go naa ezhi'aad iniwen bakwezhiganan ezhichigeyaan. Memindage naa gii-migoshkaadendaagwad apane gii-miigaading. Anaamisag gii-... gii-inoode. Obabizowebishkaan omakizineyaab abinoonjiiyens: onzaam ginwaabiigadini. Nawaj igo owenipanenimaan iniw gichi-ayaaben gaa-waabamimag iwidi noopiming. Mangate iwe abiiwigamig. Akawe ningagwinjidoon wii'-ozhitooyan mishiiminaabo. Maanamon miikana. Gii-paapaagaakwadin dibikong. Baapaagaakwadin wiiyaas. Akawe ninga-ningagwinjidoon jibwaa-giizhizamaan. Niinetawind nigii-kiiyodemin iwidi zhaaganaashiiwakiing. Niinetawind ningii-andomigoomin ji-izhaayaang iwidi odaakewigamigong. Bakaan gaye wiin odina'aan iwe nagamon gaa-noondang. Ogii-pishigonaan iw owewebanaabaan gaa-onji-bakobiisenig. Debinaak odizhitoon gaa-ozhitood wiigwaasinaagan. Ayaangwaamizin. Aapiji ozhaashikwaa iwidi ezhaayin. Agwanaatesidoon gimawinzwaanan jibwaa-baashkijiidegin. Nimbaninaan iwe onaagaans ezhi-biigosing. Gichi-anokiid naa a'aw inini gegaa gii-kawanokii. Ogii'-agaashiinyi'aan gaa-gii'-ozhitamawaad odaminwaaganensan odaanisensan. Aandi ezhiweba'ang. Mishawaagonag odizhiweba'aan bikwaakwadoons. Gijibidoon 'iw gimookomaanens. Ogii-kijibidoon 'i anwi gaa-baataashkinenig. Ogii-saagijinizhikawaan iniw abinoonjiiyan neshiwanaadakamigizinid. Ogii-kabaanizha'waan iniw ogozisan aana-gii-poozinid. Aabitoobii 'i mazhoominaaboo imaa omoodayaabikong. Ondewan iniw omoodayaabikoon. Iwidi gizhaateg akiing, agidajiw eta go gii-soogipon. Gii-kimiwan dibikong. Ingii-moona'waag mooseg gaa-ishkwaa-gimiwang. Mii igo geget gii-gichi-gimiwang. Gichi-nibiishkaamagad imaa gii-waanaskobiiyaag. Gii-kimiwan ina dibikong. Gaa-izh-mitanitewang, giga-izhi-nawajiimin; giga-nitiikemin. Iwidi neyaashiing gii-ondaasin owe jiimaan gaa-agwaayaasing. Giiwedinong ondaasin gaa-onji-gisinaag. Odagwaadaabiin onaabikwaanensiwi-jiimaan. Obwaanawitoon ji-boozid naabikwaanensiwi-jiimaan; onzaam ishpoonagadini. Gojip a'awe name. Wiinad i'iw adoopowinaak. Mii na go ji-biinitooyamban? Nitam ningii-piinitoomin indaabajichiganinaan, akikoog, miinawaa biskitenaaganan Nimbiinitoon manoomin gaa'-agwaa'oodooyaan. Nimoozhaginaanan biiwanakoonsan. Mindookad imaa mashkosiikaang inagakeyaa gaa... gaa-ni-izhaayaan wenji-dipaabaawegin nimakizinan. Niibaa-dibik ingii-nooji'aag gichi-mooseg gii-mindookak. Bakaan gaye wiin odina'aan iwe nagamon gaa-noondang. Dakoosin nagamon. Wiineta go wiin ogii-ozhitoon 'iw nagamon. Niibowa gii-izhise gii-nanaa'itood ojiimaan. Niwii-nanaa'itoon indoodaabaanens. Nimisawendaan ji-bi-nanaa'itooyamban iwe indesa'on Gii-aabitooseg ingii-onakidoon 'i bakijiiga'igan. Mii iwe wayeshkad gaa-izhichigewaad mewinzha gii-... gii-onakidoowaad waaginogaan. Gidebi' gii-pi-waabamiyan. Gii-kibaakwaji awe atoobaan gaa-onji-onzekwed aw akik indoodaabaaning. Jiikaagamin iwe aniibiish. Weweni ogii-minwaagamitoon. Gizhaabasan gitigaanensan wii'-miijiyan. Ezhi-gizii'waad iniwen owiiniskiigomaanan a'aw gwiiwizens. Indigo geget gii-gikinawaajibii'igaade. Indigo naa ge gii-ashaweyaa iwe desa'on. Indaga akawe zhingweyaabandan. Indigo naage gii-nabanetigweyaamagad 'i ziibi. Indigo gigii-wii'-ashamigoomin waabang. Ogidigamig danwewengwaamo nimishoomis. Debise 'iw maada'ookiiwin. Aaniin epiitenimad awe eshpabid. | Namanj iidog onzaam wayiiba. Onzaam wayiiba naanaagadawendaagozi. Onzaam wayiiba gii-kijigwaashkwani imaa manoominike-jiimaanensing gaa-onji-gwanabisenig. Gii-panaandawe gaa-niisaaboojiged. Gaa-naningowed igo naa 'a nebaad. Ganabaj maanaabandam. Aaniin inagakeyaa enawendiwaad. Aaniin enawendiyeg awe inini. / Agaamaya'ii niwiiji'ayaawindimin. Noosinaanig wiijikiwenyindiwag Agawaatese awe ba-desaashid giniw omaa niibawiyaan. Aandi ezhidaabaanaad. Gii-mashkawisin gaa-izhibii'iged a'aw odaake-ogimaa. Gii-pi-naaji-zagapijigaade indoodaabaanish gaa-awi-niigoseg. Nisawaatig ningii'-nibaa dibikong. Gii-chiikitaagwad biidaajimoo-mazina'igan wii'-niimi'iding. Ganabaj inga-madoodoo awaswaabang. Ingii-wiindamaag awe indoozhimikwemens wii-wiidiged awaswaabang. Gii-minwendaagoziwag omaa dibikong. Aaniish minik enangizowaad igiweg ingodooshkin opiniig. Aaniish epiichibideg. Mii na go 'i epiichibideg. Aaniin epiichibideg naabikwaanensiwi-biiwaabik. / Gaawiin igo aapiji gizhiibidesinoon. Niishtana-shi-naanan eta go apiichibide. Niin iko ningii-mimigosaga'ige gii-wiinisagaamagak 'i endaayaang. Gaawiin dakwangesii awe dinowa. Ingii-noondawaa maanashigan mamadweshing anaami-jiimaan. Odabaagamizamawaan naboob waa'-ashamaad omishoomisan. Baakaakozhan iniw biiwaabikoonsan. Ogii-pajiishkizhaanan ini biiwaabikoonsan wii-saangwewemagoodeked. Wewiib niisaandawebatoo. Onando-nakwetaan obiiwaabikoonsim madwesininig. Niga-aabaabiiginaan iwe biiminakwaan. Ganabaj owii-aabajitoonaawaa igiweg waa-shaagoojibinidiwaad. Waawiiba omeshkojisidoon gaa-ozhibii'igesenig odoozhibii'iganaakong. Ningaabii'anong ondwewidamoog animikiig gii-bimwewidamowaad. Gegaa ogii-nisaan iniwen ingaazhagensiminaan noozhishenh. Dagwamaadaa bakwezhigan. Ningii-noonde-gimiwanish gii-bi-giiweyaan. Ningiikadaabaawe. Bi-anokiin. Bwaanawichige a'aw inini ji-anokiipan. Aaniish wenji-aanizhiitaman megwaa anokiiyimban. Biisiboojiganing niwii'-anokii biboong. Ninookab. Gabeya'ii geyaabi ninga-anokii. Bijiinaago gii-maajitaa. Giinitam gigii'-maajitaa. Ogii-mazinaakizaan i'iw indooshkidaabaan. Aanikoopidewan makakosagodaabaanan. Aanjiwidoon iwe. Awas iwidi izhiwidoon. Aandi ezhiwidood. Ishpimisagong izhiwidoon. Ziinziningwaandan ji-izhiwidooyin. Niwii-izhiwidoon iwidi indoodaabaan noomaabikinigan ji-aanjichigaadeg. Nookomis odoozaawegizaan odasekaan. Omooshkineyaabasaan Gichi-niibiwa imaa aana-gii-abi a'aw mikwam. Mii zhigwa biinish igo ani-... ani-angwiid. Abinoojiinyag agindaasowag bezhig biinish igo ningodwaak. Biinish igo gii-ani-onaagoshig geyaabi ingii-pawa'aamin. Gaa-gizhiibideg naabikwaanens ningii'-adaawen waa'-aabajitoowaan ando-mawinzowaan noongom gaa-niibing Mamaazhiish igo naa izhi-nawadanjige. Ombiigwewebizonike awe medwe-daashkiboojiged. Ogii-piisiga'aanaawaa i'iw mishi. Mii na go 'iw ji-gashkitooyegiban ji-ozhitooyeg bakejiigaan? | Enh, ninitaawichigemin. Gii-webaasin i'iw babiinzikawaagan omaa aana-gii-agoodooyaan. Weweni mamoon. Aapiji ozhaashadamon. Nimazinigwaadaan i'iw babagiwayaan. O'owe inagakeyaa gidaa-inagoodoon ni-waabanjigaadegiban. Zinigojiibizh giday. Andookomaazh. Indawaaj naa apii igo inga-o-giishkikoz. Niwenda-gagaanwaanikwe. Aabitooshkinewag igiw mandaamini-gaapizigaansag imaa booskinaaganing. Nimanezin niizhooshkin 'i bingwi. Zhebaa ogii'-wiinaan ge-izhi-anishinaabewinikaazonid. Miiwan iniwe wiiyawen'enyan. Ingaagiidiz imbikwanaang. Miziwe gaagiidizi gaa-izhishimoonod gii-kwanabibizod bijiinaago. Giwii-kizhaakiganez ina. Gii-ishkwaa-gidasigaadeg i'iw manoomin, mii zhigwa gii-mimigoshkigaadeg. Giishpin ganage bebangii diba'aman gidoodaabaan, ingoding igo giga-giizhi-diba'aan. Giishpin Jason de-diba'ang waasigani-bimide, waabang da-bagamibizo. Niwii-izhaa ashangewigamigong. Ingii-shaashaagwamaa awe wiikenh gechi-aakwaadizid. Gegaa gii-kawajiwag igi animoonsag gaa-izhi-biindiganagwaa. Aapiji gisinaa, mii go wenda-gawajiyaan. Ozhichigaade waa-tazhi-madoodooyang. Gii'-ozhibii'igaazowag minik waa'-anokiitamowaad waakaa'igan gaa-wii'-ozhichigaadeg. Gaawiin giiyaabi gizhibaawebinigaadesinoon odaabaanan,. Mewinzha ko gaa-... gii-... gii-izhichigaadewan Mii iniw en... enokiitawaad waabishkiiwenid gaa-oshki-bagamised. Ishkwaaj gaa-gii'-anokiitawagiban, aapiji gii'-minwaadizi. Ningitiziimag nindanokiitawaag. Giishpin madwesidood nimbiiwaabikoonsim, ninga-gagwejimaa ji-anokiitawag. Niimi'iding ningii-izhaamin gii-anama'e-giizhigak. Mii iwidi gii-kabeshiyaang. Apishimoniken ininaandagoog ozhitooyan giwiigiwaam. Aaniin ekwaabiigizid gizenibaam gaa-naabishimad. Gwekiwebin igiweg gwekiwebiniganag. Gwekiwebinaa mii 'i wenji-izhinikaazod "gwekwebinigan." Biinzaabam akik. Mii go 'i gii-kiizhendamowaad igi giigidoowininiwag waa-izhichigewaad. Mii na 'iw gii-kiizhendaman inagakeyaa waa-izhi-biinjwebinigeyan. Bijiinaago gii-maajitaa. Gii-aakwendam gaa-izhishing gii-pangishing bijiinaago. Gii-maazhi-giizhigad bijiinaago gaa-onji-bwaanawitooyaan ji-gopiiyaan. Bijiinaago niibiwa ningii-kaaskizaan wiiyaas. Noongom idash niwii'-nooka'iiwagwe. Baamaa bengwaandagaag giga-manaanzhidemin; onzaam nibiiwaandagaa 'owapii. Nimisawendam ji-gichi-ozhooniyaamiyaan ingonding. I'imaa gaa-onjiiyaan apane go anishinaabemowag. Aapiji gii-sanagadini i'imaa gaa-tazhi-mitanokiid. Aandi enaadagaaziid. Anaamikwam iko ningii-pagida'waamin. Ogii-pimijishimaan odasabiin awe gaa-'o-bagida'waad. Onaazibiiwinaan odasabiin waa'-ando-bagida'waad. Gii-ishkwaangewag gaa-onji-aabidanokiiwaad. Gegaa gii-pizikawaa anishaa go niin gaa-ikowebinag. Ogii-ikowebinaan iniwen gwiiwizensan jibwaa-bizikoozonid. Gipagishin awe waabigan endanaanikeyin. Weweni ogii-oninaan iniw waabiganan. Ogii-nookibinaan ini waabiganan waa-aabaji'aad. Ajina ningii-mawadisaa nishiime. Gagwaanisa ajina gii-pimaaboojige aana-gii-gichi-ozhooniyaamid. Ajina eta ingii-tazhitaamin gii-wiisiniyaang. Ajina go ningii-kaganoonaa jibwaa-boozid gichi-odaabaanan. Ajina go noongom mbi-anokii. Giishpin asekaadaman bashkwegin, biinish da-ani-nookiigad. Agwaawebinan gigiishka'isaanan biinji-naabikwaanensiwi-jiimaaning gaa-ategin. Ogii-panoomaan obimoonjiganan. Gii-piigwaashi 'aw bimoonjigan. Baakagoojin awe imbimoonjigan. Noondaadiwag, gaawiin idash waabandanziiwag. Mooshkine-awan 'i ziibi. Agaami-ziibi danwewidam. Megwaa go zhiibid gaa-izhi-ojibinigogaaded. Gii-gichi-ojibinigogaade wenji-gaagiijigaaded awe bemibatood. Minwendaagwad igo aanawi zhooshkonigeng giishpin bakinaageng. Ogii-o-gikatoon 'i nibaashkizhiganish aw mindimooyenh waa-onji-zhooshkoniged. Nibiiwiziwag igi wazhashkwedowensag. Gidaa-wiisookawaag apane gichi-anishinaabeg. Gegoo imaa giga-onji-gikendaan ge-ani-izhi-mino-bimaadiziyan. Nindaanis obiizikaanan oshkiinzhigokaanan odaabii'iwed. Gaawiin aapiji waabisiin. Giwii-piizikaan ina iwe babagiwayaan gemaa... gemaa go iwedi. Ogigishkaan nibabiinzikawaagan aana-wii-piizikamaan. Biizikan ginamekwaanakizinan. Nibiiwashkosiwagaa agwajiing. Ogii-tipaabaawadoon owiiwakwaan jibwaa-biizikang; onzaam abwezo. Gii-maazhichige gii-bakwebidood i'iwe apakwaan. Aandi ezhidaabii'iwed. Nookomis endaad indizhidaabii'iwe. Niizhoopizowag animoshag gaa-odaabii'aad gaa-maa'ishkang. Wiinge gizhiiwewebide nindoodaabaanish. Ganabaj bagwaabikishkaa gaa-onji-zaagidaabateseg. Bagwaabikishkaa gwaaba'iganish wenji-onjigaag. Gaawiin ganage indaa-biinjwebinigetamowaasii awe gemoodishkid. Gaawiin giiyaabi gizhibaawebinigaadesinoon odaabaanan,. Mewinzha ko gaa-... gii-... gii-izhichigaadewan Giwiidabindimin gii-anokaadamang anishinaabe-ikidowinan. Aaniin epiichiid gaa-anokaadang waakaa'igan. Zhigwa na odapakwaadaan. Agaaming wii-izhi-goziwag. Gego indawaaj gozisiidaa. Zhebaa gii-pimi-zaagidawa'owag gaa-andawawinzowaad. Gakiiwewidaaso gaa'-ishkwaa-wanii'iged. Wii'-ani-zaagidawa'o wii'-ani-giiwed. Aaniin ezhiigak. Wa'a giniin naa ge baadaasamigaabawid abinoonjii. Wenda-wiinaabiigizi. Awenenag igiwedig? Giiwedaabaazh amik gaa-gii-tasoonad. Giishpin dasoonad zhagashkaandawe, azhe-biinjiwebin makakoonsing. Mii awe gigokeyaw. Niwenda-gwiinawi-inanaam; onzaam gizhide. Daga wiindamaw ji-ni-giiwed 'a gwiiwizens. Ojibwemonodaw go weweni ji-wiindamowad iwe ge-izhichiged. Gii-kwiinawi-inendam gii-pi-wiindamawind gichi-aakozinid ookomisan. Giishpin ondamiziyan, niin giga-ozhibii'igetamawin. Wiindamawishin waa'-ikidoyan. Gego memwech wiindamawaaken. Aazha ogikendaan waa'-izhichiged. Owii-madwe'waan iidog odewe'iganiman awaswaabang. Iwidi ogidakamig ate 'iw endawaabandaman. Onjida go gagiibaazinaagozi awe gizhenaabens zhoomiingwenid. Gego gakina zaagijibinaaken zhooniyaa izhaayan zhooniyaawigamigong. Ishkonamawishin. Mii zhigwa oditang gichi-aya'aawiwin. Gii-ani-giiwe-biboong biniwinewag waawaashkeshiwag, gaye moozoog. Bezhig eta ogii-ni-maajiinaan ini akikoon awe naadaabowed. Ajina eta ingii-tazhitaamin gii-wiisiniyaang. Aanind eta go. Bebangii eta go. Gitigaanensan eta go gii-inadaawaage. Bagakaasige 'aw giizis. Bagakaasigewag anangoog. Gichi-bagakaasige awe dibiki-giizis aana-aabitawaabikizid. Mii ko ingiw ikwewag naadamaagewaad nagamong mii imaa zhaabowewaad ezhi-wiinjigaadeg. Giwiidabindimin gii-anokaadamang anishinaabe-ikidowinan. Ogii-piinitamowaan odoopwaaganan. Ogii-miikwa'aan 'i bikwaakwad awe bagitejii'igewinini. Igiw bagitejii'igewininiwag ogii-aabiinji'aawaan iniw gaa-pi-mawine'ogowaad gii-pi-ataagowaad. Agaawaa deba'oode zaga'igan; onzaam michaabikad. Gaawiin igo aapiji inzaazaabiisii. Mii zhigwa adimigooyaan awe gikaawin. Niigaan ani-maajaan. Booch giga-adimigoo. Ningii'-adimaa gaa-mikinaaked. Ogii-mazinibii'aan indengwaan 'a gwiiwizhenzhish. Gigikenimaa na awe gwiiwizens. Wawiingeziwag igiw gwiiwizensag manisewaad. Gakina ogii'-ombwewebinaa' nindakikoo' gii-naganag 'a gwiiwizenzhish. Gidatoon ina ziinzibaakwad imaa ginitiiming. Ginibise 'iw ziinzibaakwad. Niwii-naadin midaaso-dibaabiishkoojigan iwe ziinzibaakwad. Aa, gaawiin ji-miijiyaan ziinzibaakwad. Ziinzibaakwad ina giwii-tagonaan. Ningii-izhaamin iko gagiikwewigamigong gii-pizindawangid awe gagiikwewinini gagiikwed. Gii-o-gagiikwe nisayenh imaa gikinoo'amaadiiwigamigong. O'owe inagakeyaa odinagoonaan. Endaso-ziigwan niwazhashkwanii'ige. Wa'a giniin naa ge baadaasamigaabawid abinoonjii. Wenda-wiinaabiigizi. Gego mashi biindigeken. Geyaabi nibiiwisagaa. Noongom nindishkwaa-giziisaginige. Baapaawaange maang gii-mooshkamod. Indaga niizhozid biidamawishin awe mekadewaabiigizid zenibaa. Biizh awe mekadewaabiigizid asabaabiins. Mekadewaabiigizid zenibaa gidaa-dagwapikaazonan. Naniizaanendam ji-ipizonikepan imaa gichi-oodenaang. Ginwenzh ingii-inendimin gii-izhaayaang gichi-oodenaang. Gii-nibekaazo gii-megwaa-animikiikaag. Omegwaa-ningizaan 'i wiinin a'aw mindimooyenh. Giishpin apane miikindizid da-moo'aa wiiba. Giiyaabi go gigizhebaawagad. "Maagizhaa gii-ishkwaa-naawakwe," indinendam. Agaami-oodena izhi-ando-wiisinidaa. Gii-tibiki-bimwewebiisaa. Giishpin ningwakwak, wiiba wii'-niiskaadad. Onzaam wiiba ningii'-amaji'igoo zhebaa. Giishpin ningizigodeg, wiiba gigizheb giga-gagwe-aazhawagaakomin. Mii go gakina ezhi-minookamiiwaad igiweg baaga'adowewaad. Gakina nibaawag omaa eyaawaad. Zhaawanong gakina izhaawag niibiniseg gii-dagwaagig. Ikwanaamose gii-wiindamawag ezhiwebizinid odedeyan. Mii 'i zhigwa z...  maadaawadaasod awe zaagijigidaazod Mii gii-maajiikang iwe bakejiigaan wezhitood. Weweni go inaajimo. Bakaan inaajimo awedi bezhig apiich idash wa'awe. Aanind ogaadoon enaajimod. Gaawiin gakina dibaajimosii. Ogii-ozaawaakizwaan iniw giboziganan waa-amwaad. Awenen waa'-ozaawaakizwaad giboziganan. Midaaswi awiyag gidaa-ashamaanaanig. Nimookawaadaan nindanokiiwin. Ningii'-wanitoon. Giinetawaa izhaag iwidi andomigooying. Giinetawaa na gigii-nisidotaam? Giinetawaa gigikenimininim nitaa-aagimikeyeg. Waabang wii'-na'inigaazo gaa-gii'-ishkwaa-ayaad. Gii-gichi-onzaamiino goon gii-biboonagak. Obaapaawa'aan goonan. Mii imaa ogijayi'ii odaabaaning a goon abid. Gagiizhibaayaashi goon. Baapaawin 'a goon maa gibabiinzikawaaganing. Gibaakwa'an ishkwaandem. Biindigeyaashi goon. Ningii-maniwiigwaasemin iko niinawind nimaamaayiban. Niinawind iko nimisenyiban ingii-agoodinasabiimin. Gaye niinawind ingii-izhaamin endanataading. Indaga zaagizi' a'aw animosh ji-babaamosa'ad. Ingii-piindige imaa endazhi-adaawaageng iniw waabigwaniin. Minomaagwad imaa biindig. "Gichi-minomaagwadoon ini waabigwaniin gaa-piidamawiyin," odinaan iniw onaabeman a'a ikwe. Nimaamaa ogii-aabajitoon mashkawaji-bimide gii-ombigamiziged ji-ziigigamidesinok iwe odoombigamizigan. Baashkijiise i'iw apikweshimon. Gichi-ombiigizi awe megadeshkid. Giishpin baasindibenawad amik, aabita-diba'igan izhiseg da-aabooshkanjise. Aaniin endasingin. Aaniin endasing iwe ziinzibaakwad. Mii iw gii-moona'waad iniw odoopiniiman Niibinong ningii-gitigaanaanaanig opiniig. Naanginigoziwag igiweg opiniig imaa baanzowaad mashkimodaang. Bakwezhiganaaboo niwii-tagonaan indoopiniiming. Ozaasagokwaan opiniin a'aw nookomis. Zaasagokwaanagwaa opiniing nindagozwaag zhigaagawanzhiig. Omaamiginaan iniw odoopiniiman. Gichi-noonde-nibaayaan gaa-izhi-gawishimoyaan wii-nibaayaan. Geyaabi nimbakade. Gichi-bakadeyaan naa gegaa naa ingii-kawanaandam. Gegapii go ani-bakade. Gegaa go gaawiin ninisidawinawaasii awe niitaawis. Nawaj noongom bakade. Gaawiin geyaabi ogashki'aasiin ji-bimibizo'aad odaabaanan; onzaam gaawiin zaabaabisii. Ogii-kashki'aan iniwen odikweman ji-wiijiiwigod iwidi zagaswe'iding ji-izhaawaad. Onaazitaan baawitig endanwewejiwaninig. Miziwe danwewejiwan gii-ziigwang. Ishkwaase anokiiwin. Giga-mikamawin anokiiwin. Ogii-naabishkawaan odanokiiwin gaa-giiwoodenid. Mashi na gigii-maajitoon gidanokiiwin. Onjikadan gidanokiiwin gidoozhibii'igewigamigong. Omiigaadaan odanokiiwin ji-ganawendang. Biidoog iniwen biizikiganan. Naawisag-sh imaa giga-atoonaawaan. Naawisag gii-kawishimo 'a nindaanis. Mii imaa gii-padakijigaadeg adoopowinaak imaa naawisag. Giwii-adaam ina. Ingii-adaamaa ditibidaabaanan gaa-ayaad. Mii go booch gii-piindigadood odoozhibii'igan misawaa go aana-gii-inind ji-aanizhiitang. Nizhawenimaa a'aw inini misawaa go aana-gii-bakinawid. Biindigen. Gego memwech madweyaakwa'igeken. Aazha misawaa gigii'-waabamin. Gii-pagoshkaa 'aw atoobaan gaa-onji-iskigaad. Azhiwaa na gimoozhwaagan. Agwaabidoon giniminaawaandawaagan jibwaa-gashkading. Gegaa go gaawiin ninisidawinawaasii awe niitaawis. Nawaj noongom bakade. Bezhig nawaj zhaangaso minik midaaswi. Nawaj gozigwan iwe ashkikomaan apiich idash iwe biiwaabik. Jiigitawag gidaa-ganoonaa. Nawaj igo gagiibishe Nawaj bekaa ikidon. Mangitoon nawaj i' ishkwaandem imaa ataasoowigamigong. Nawaj gaanda'amiidaa. Giga-nagajibizomin ishkodewidaabaan. Zhaawanong gii-izhidooneni. Gii-tajise awe odaabii'iwewinini gaa-onji-giiwenizha'ond. Gigii-aanjidaabaane. Wawiinge go gigichi-mazina'ige miinawaa. Ingii-aanjidaabane biboonong. Aaniin apii waa'-aanjidaabaaneyan. Agwajiing ningii-izhaa, gaa-izhi-giikajizidewajiyaan, gaa-izhi-biindigeyaan gii-kiizikamaan nimakizinan. Oo yaay zegitaagwad. Miinooj igo niwii-odaabii'iwe ani-dibikak. Miinooj ninga-gagwejimaa nindoogimaam ji-ishpi-diba'amawid nawaj. Miinooj igo niwii-o-ataage. Miinooj iidog ninga-gagwejimaa. Aaniin enaadizid? Gwayak ina inaadizi ji-debwetawindiban. Gidaa-onzwaa na awe giingoo. Nindoonzwaag miskojiisiminag. Niwii-shaabonaan owe mitigoons. Nakwebidoon iwidi waabandaman. Ogii-kwekinaan aana-gii-nanaa'isijigaadenig 'i waasechiganaabik. Niikimo a' animosh. Ganabaj awiya odamanisodawaan. Onowe gidaa-biisikaanan azhiganan. Biiniigadoon onowe. Giin ina onowe gimazina'iganan. Gii-shagashkii gii-gaagiimaa'aad zhiishiiba'. Baatayiinogaade wa'awe manidoosh. Gaawiin wiikaa ingii'-odaminwaagesiinag manidooshag. Gaawiin gidaa-dakwamigosii awe manidoosh. Inigaayendaagoziwag igiweg manidooshag aana-nanaamadabiyaan imaa agwajiing. Ogii-minotaan i'iw nagamoo-makakoons gaa-onji-adaawed. Onaazibiiwinaan odasabiin waa'-ando-bagida'waad. Ginwaabiigizhan zhinoodaagan waa'-wewebizonikaageyan. Ningii'-agozideshkawaa wanakozid. Enendam jigijigaaneshiinh wiikojitood ge-miijid. Aaniin epiitanid bezhigwaatig giikanaabate-gookoosh. Giinitamawaa ina giga-wiidookaazom ji-manashkosiweng. Giinitamawaa awi-maniseg. Giinitamawaa bakwezhiganikeyok. Odaabaanaak aabadizi gegoo gii-naajidaabiing. Dabasigaabawiwan omishtadimoonsiman gaa-debasaanaad. Gegaa gii-pizikawaa anishaa go niin gaa-ikowebinag. Gabe-biboon noopimiing ningiishka'aakwe. Gabe-biboon iwidi gii-anokii nishiime. Gaawiin dash geyaabi anokiisiin Gabe-biboon biindig indayaa. Don ogii'-wiiji-wanii'igemaan oosan gabe-biboon. Zanagizi bezhig awe inday. Aapiji goshkokaa. Giga-zanagizimin ji-gawiboojigeying noongom; onzaam mashkawaanimad. Zanagizi wii-tebibinind 'a mishtadim. Gigagiibaadendaagoz. Gagwe-minjiminan iwe gaa-izhi-onagimigooyin imaa gii-piinjwebinigeng. Noongom ogowe abinoojiinyag onapaazikaanaawaan owiiwakwaaniwaan, gaye obiimishkaanaawaan. Giishpin mikwaminaaniwang, waabowayaan gidaa-badagwana'waa gidoodaabaan ji-maakishkoozosig. Aaniish enanokiiyin. Mii go eyiizh enanokiiyaang. Ondaas igo ondaadad i'iw od... odaabaan gaa-adaaweyaan. Midaaso-biboon gii-ondaadad indoodaabaanish. Aandi enaandawed. Dibaabam odaabaanag jibwaa-azhebizoyan. Azhebizon ji-bakwajibidegin anzaziin. Niwiijibizoomaa nindaanis gii-booziyaan gaa-gizhibaabideg. Niizhiwag niniijaanisag. Ningii-kanawenimaa a'aw biibiiyens omaamaayan gii-maa'ishkaminid. Aapiji niganawenimig awe niwiijiiwaagan ji-noondendanziwaan. Ganawenim a'awe. Gimoodaatigweshki. Gikinawaajibii'an indaga owe gaa-ozhibii'igaadeg. Eyiidawishkiinzhig odaabajitoon ziiginiingwaan. Gagwe-minjimishkan iwe biiminakwaan ezhi-zagapideg iwidi mizhasiniing. Ingii-piminizhikawaa inday gaa-niimandang niwiiwakwaan. Ogii-mazinibii'aan indengwaan 'a gwiiwizhenzhish. Agwaasidoon gijiibaakwaan jibwaa-agwaabikideg. Anooj igo ogii-izhinaagotoon 'o omazinikojigan. Mii gaa-izhinaagotood gaa-anoonag ji-ozhiitood 'iw gibaakwa'igan. Anaami-adoopowin ayaa a'aw animosh migid. Biindig dazhi-migi awe ninday. Madwe-migi. Onandomaamaan awe inday iniw gaa-pi-odishiyangid dibikong. Gabe-giizhik gashkaabate. Ganabaj ingoji zakide. Naano-diba'igaans gii-kaazhipoose niso-diba'iganek. Ogii-azheyaabika'waan ini diba'igeziswaanan naano-diba'igaans. Giishpin mashkawaabiigak ginagwaaganeyaab, naano-diba'igaans akawe miskwaabikizan waa'-izhi-biskaabikinaman. Nimaamaa ogii-aabajitoon mashkawaji-bimide gii-ombigamiziged ji-ziigigamidesinok iwe odoombigamizigan. Indaabaji'aa akik naadoobiiyaan. Jiigishkode nindagoonaa a'aw akik ozhitooyaan naboob. Madwe'ige 'aw akik indoodaabaaning. Mii i'iw ganabaj ji-zhaabonikesed. Gakina ogii'-ombwewebinaa' nindakikoo' gii-naganag 'a gwiiwizenzhish. Aakwaasige 'aw giizis. Aabitawaabikizi 'aw giizis. Bangishimo 'aw giizis. Gizhaasige awe giizis. Miinange ninga-gashkitoon ji-ozhitoowaan. Ingii-pazhinanig awe inday gii-paashkigidaazod. Agwinaanan ogigishimonan. Gizhiibani'o oshkiniigikwe agwinaanan gaa-agwiid. Wiikaa ko nimbi-ganoonig nishiimenh. Wiikaa gii-pi-dagoshin indaanis. Wiikaa na bizaan-ayaa. Naadwewendiwag gaa-andonizhikigewaad. Obabizowebishkaan omakizineyaab abinoonjiiyens: onzaam ginwaabiigadini. Ninganawaabandaan iko iwe mazinaatesijigan. Mii imaa mazinaakizowaad igi ininiwag maagizhaa ikwewag waanda-... waanda-gichi-wiininowag naa. Wenda-biinge-waabishkindibe awe gichi-aya'aa. Wii-maawanji'iidiwag igiw gichi-aya'aag wii-tazhindamowaad mewinzha gaa-pi-izhiwebak. Onji'o gichi-aya'aa ji-izhichigewind. Gegapii go nawaj ani-niminaawekii manoomin. Ogiji-nibewin daningwaamo bizhiins. Mii iwidi niibidesingin biizikiganan ogijaya'ii. Ogijaya'ii imaa nibaaganing. Ishte. Webinigan naa wa'aw baandiged. Gichi-michiigizi awe bashkwegin. Akawe weweni ando-gikendan jibwaa-baashkizaman. Akawe gidaa-bagidinaan; onzaam gozigwan. Ogii-gikinawaajitoon imaa gaa-ni-izhaad megwekob ji-wanishinzig. Megwekob iwidi gii-izhi-gwaashkwesin 'iw bikwaakwad. Megwekob imaa ingii-andawaabandaanan miinan. Megwekob imaa ngii-pabaa-bakiteshin. Babaamishkaa 'a akiwenzii anwaatininig. Awibaamagad, gichi-anwaatin igaye. Gegapii go ani-maadaanimad aana-gii-anwaating. Ani-giiwen. Biinizikaa gaa-ni-izhi-giiwed nindaanis. Ingii-inaa ji-giiwed. Ozhinawisidamawaan. "Ambe gaazhagens bi-giiwen." Niiwing naa gii-maadanjige ningozis. Niiwing ningii-pi-gabadoomin gii-bi-nita'amaang. Awasaatig iwidi owi-gaazon. Anaamaya'ii imaa adoopowining ingii-kaazomin. Anishinaabewanjigewag geyaabi gaa-onji-mino-ayaawaad. Ogii-saagijinizhikawaan iniw abinoonjiiyan neshiwanaadakamigizinid. Gii-naabidoo'amaan i'iw zhaabonigan, ningii-kashka'oonaa a'aw asabaabiins. Ogii-noonishkaanan aana-gii-kozikang iniwen makizinan a'awe nindaanis. Biindikomaaning zhegonan gimookomaan jibwaa-beshininjiishinan. Ogii-bishigwa'aan iwe aana-wii-kaanda'ang jiimaan gaa-onji-bakobiised. Aandi wenjijiwang. Gii-o-adaawetamaage waa-aabajichigaadenig o'o waa-inakamigak Ogii-kibishkaan iwe miikana awe gaag gii-megwaa-aazhawishkaad. Gaag obishagaakwamaa' mitigoo'. Giishpin okawi'ad awiya wawaaga'amiid, gaag a'a gaa-bimikawed. Onjikadan gidanokiiwin gidoozhibii'igewigamigong. Gii-kiikibii'ige aw asigibii'igewinini aana-gikendaasod. Indaga naa asham a'awe. Mii gosha go naa wenda-waabiiganaandang. Niwii-kiziibiigizide jibwaa-agonjidooyaan inzidan imaa gichi-onaaganing. Inoo'amaw inakeya'ii ge-izhi-onabid. Ogodaagaminaan nibi epiitaagamidenig. Owanakoninj odaabajitoon. Mishawaagonag odizhiweba'aan bikwaakwadoons. Dakisijiganing izhi-atoon gaa-gii'-ishkwandaman ji-wanaajisinzinog. Dazhi-agwaanaaso gaa-gii'-maa'ishkang. Gii-kichi-adaawe. Giishpin andone'ang anokiiwin, oga-mikaan. Babaa-aazhawaakwii-gwaashkwani waabizheshi andone'ang waa'-miijid. Enigok gii-wiikwii. Gaawiin gegoo naanaagadawendanziin awe gaa-onji-bakiiwiid aw gaa-wiikwiid. Ogii-odaapizwaan iniw odewe'iganan -- onzaam jiigayi'ii iwidi ogii-minjiminaan jiigishkodeng. Amik giinwanaamo. Gabeya'ii jibwaa-mooshkamod. Baapaawaange maang gii-mooshkamod. Mii 'i zhigwa ani-gashkiidibikak, giiyaabi go waasete abiiwigamig. Wiiba noongom ani-gashkiidibikad. Miidog 'i zhigwa ani-ishpi-dagwaagig. Naawi-minis debinaagwad migiziwazison. Mii idi neyaashiing wenjiwijiged imaa bemiwidood ini jiimaanan. Gii'-nookijiishkaani gaa-ditibisenig odaabaaning, mii iwe gaa-onji-bezikaad. Anaamidaabaaning zhegoshin nanaa'idaabaaned. Dibikong nimaamaa gii-pi-zhegoshing ninibewining. Ishkwe-minis iwidi giga-ozhigemin, giga-izhi-gabeshimin. Ogidadoopowinaak ashi gibakwezhiganikaan. Jiigishkode onji-giizhizwi gibakwezhiganikaan. Aasamishim. Godigoshin imaa odinimaanganaang. Gichi-waawaashkeshiwan ogii-mikonizhikawaan. Minisinadaawangaang danaamiwag giigoonyag. Mii ji-bwaanawi'ad ji-gichiwinadiban. Ojaanimendam wii-azhegiiwed iwidi gaa-pi-onji-bazigwiid gaa-izhiwebadinig. Aaniin enaanimak. Akawe waabandan enaanimak jibwaa-aazhawa'oyan. Gii-mashkawaabiigad i'iw zhinoodaagan gaa-aabajichigaadeg gii-dakobinind a'aw asab. Ganabaj wiiba da-bwaanawi'o nimishoomis. Mashkikiiwininiwan odigoon okanaapined. Aaniin ekwaabiigakin gimakizineyaabiin. Diba'iganaaakoons aabajitoon wii-kikendaman ekwaabiigak. Mii 'iwe zhigwa bapangishinowaad igiweg mishiiminag. Opime-aya'ii waakaa'iganing atewan iniwen misan. Nigashkiwinaag ogow asabiig...  aanawi. Gii-memeshkwajiiwag igi gaa-azhebowewaad gii-aazhawa'oodoowaad iwe jiimaan imaa zaaga'iganing. Onzaam ginwaabikad iwe gaandakii'igan miinawaa onzaam gozigwan. Awenen wejiimaanid. Giishpin minjimaakwiisiwan, giga-bishigwaakwii. Ogidaagonag iwidi animibatoo aw zhingos. Ogidaagonag izhi-asham bineshiinyensag. Ogidaagonag iko ingii-odaminomin. Mii go bijiinag gii-mamayaawiiwaad midaaso-diba'iganeg zhebaa. Onzaam gabaya'ii gii-agoojin  'a bashkwegin gaa-onji-bigishkananid. Boodaashkaa waawaashkeshi; onzaam gabeyi'ii agoojin mitigong. Gichi-michaabikizi awe dibiki-giizis egoojing. Aaniish minik imaa egoojinowaad. Mii zhigwa wayiiba ji-giizhiged awe waakaa'iged. Mii imaa ataagewigamigong endanendaagozid. Jiigishkwaand namadabin. Ogii-padakinaa' odaagima' jiigishkwaand. Bemijigamaag ningii-izhaamin. Ningii-naajimiijimemin. Gabe-giizhik ningii-ondendimin. Gichi-noodin wenji-gichi-wewebaasing i'iw okikiwe'on. Gii-wewebaasin iwe ogikiwe'on. Ginwaakwad gikiwe'on gaa-izhi-wewebaasing Indaashaayok. Boozig omaa. Niwii-pooz imaa biinjidaabaan. Ogii-kiboobidoon iw ogashkibidaagan jibwaa-boozid imaa ishkodewidaabaaning. Nitam nimbooz imaa jiimaaning awi-bagida'waayaang. Bebesho badakidewan iniw wiigiwaaman. Gaa-izhi-miigaadiwaad igiw niizh abinoojiinyag, mii dash awe gikinoo'amaagewikwe ogii-kaganoonaan. Ingii-wii-anokiimin iwidi St. Paul gii-pi-angizod awe aabita-niibino-giizis. Mii miinawaa wiiba ji-odisaabamang awe aabita-niibino-giizis. Nindaanis ningii-pi-ashamig odishkwanjiganiwaa. Gidaa-ashamaa giday gidishkwanjigan. Ginwaabiigigwe waabizii. Zhigwa bagakinaagwad mii 'i gaa-ishkwaa-awang. Nitaa-ojibwemowag igi abinoojiinyag gekinoo'amawindwaa iwidi Waadookodaading. Ojibwemo noongom awe gaa-waabamag zhaaganaashiiwanishinaabe. Gidaa-gii-pina'ige jibwaa-bagamibiisaang. Gagiipizi eyedawidooskwan. Awegonen waandamaagegwen awe ikwe. Giishpin gashkitooyan, gidaa-ojibwewibii'ige ji-wiindamaageyin aaniin apii ge-zagaswe'idiing. Wegonen apane wenji-nishkaaji-giigidod gidede. Ingii-nishki'ig gaa-onji-gichi-basiingwe'wag. Giishpin odaminwaagesiwan bikwaakwad, da-ani-nookijiishkaa. Waabiganikaadeni onik. Bijiinag miinawaa ani-ziigwang gii-saagibagaag ji-mazhii'igewaad igiweg anokiiwininiwag. Nimayaawibani' jibwaa-waabamigooyaan. Zhiishiibag bimaadagaawag. Noondese maada'ookiiwin. Gidaa-biidoonan niizh apabiwinan. Noondesewan. Akawe wii'-apatoo adaawewigamigong. Noondese doodooshaaboo. Baaka'aakwenhwigamigoonsing iwidi apane owi-asiginang iniw waawanoon. Wiikwaasinjigan aabajitoon wii-chiishada'igeyan. Wiikwaasinoon gaa-biiwisingin michisag. Mii iniw gaa-nisigod wadowan. Gichi-apiitendaagozi awe wemitigoozhiiwasimoons waa-adaaweyin. Aaniin epiitagoodooyan gima'iingani-nagwaaganan. Agaaming iwidi ningii'-onjikadaan bezhig nindabwi. Gagaanwaakwadoon abwiin. Giishpin agaasaakwak gidabwi, giga-bookobidoon nita'aman. Ogotaan ji-aazhawishkang iwe gete-aazhoganish. Ogii-mikomaan iniw ogete-wiiwan. Gete-anishinaabeg wiidoopandiwag. Odaabiskobidoon gete-zhiibiigishkaawayaanish. Owii'-aabajitoon miskogaadeyaab. Andodamaageshki gaa-nakweshkawag ikwe bijiinaago. Giishpin gashkitooyan, webikodan iwe wadikwaans. Gaye niinawind ingii-izhaamin endanataading. Gii-aazhawibizo imaa eshpaanig aazhogan. Niwiidanokiimaagan dakoonagiziwan odoodaabaanan. Memeshkwad gii-kaakaadoowag ogow gaa-makizinataagewaad. Gii-ombwebidewan ini mitigoonsan gii-pingwa'ogooyaang gii-megwaa-makizinataageyaang. Gaa-izhi-neyaabikaanig bi-onji-agwaakawewag. Ozhiitaawag igiw mewine'igewaad. Mii azhigwa makadekewaad. Azhigwa ngiikiibingwash. Mii go bijiinag noongom gigizhebaawiiyaan owe giziibiigisaginigewi-giizhigak. Indaga o-baapaawa'an iwe apishimon. Mazinigwaasowag igi ikwewag. Wewebizowag igi abinoonjiiyag imaa wewebizoning. Ningii-pishigonaa a' zhooniyaans imaa mitaamik. Mii go 'iw gegaa baasi-biigoshkaayaan mii eta go aabitawaabik eyaawag. Ogii-naaji-zagaabiiginaan odayan. Aaniin epiitendaagwak gidikidowin. Ge niinawind ningii'-aanikanootaamin ikidowinan. Gii-miinigoowizi gakina gegoo ji-nisidotang ikidowinan. Ominosidoon odikidowin. Anaamaabik ogii-izhi-gaanaan ozhooniyaaman. Zhebaa nitam gii'-oda'amii nindaanisens. Ogii-taangishimaan bebezhig gii-asaad iniw wezaawiminagizinid. Giziibweweshkaa 'iw ishkwaandemish. Indaga noomaabikinan. Nindooshki-aanikoobijiganens jiikinaagozi; mamaanganowe. Gezhibaayaaniwanook izhinikaazo. Bijiinag apii ninga-nakwetawaa. Mii 'iw bijiinag gii-nanaa'endang gaa-oko-gwayakobii'igaadenig obiindigajigan. Bijiinag goziikang. Mii 'iw bijiinag gii-pazigwiiwaad gaa-kidaanawewaad igiw abinoonjiiyag. Bijiinag naagaj waaswaakang: onzaam oshki-dibikad. Bijiinag ninga-gikendaan ge-izhitooyaan. Bijiinag igo biidaabang giga-bakinasabiimin. Ishkwaabiisaag, bijiinag giga-niminaawa'omin. Dawisin i'iw odaabaaniiwigamig. Nametoo imaa odaabaaniiwigamigong gii-andawaabanjigegwen. Gegaa ningii-pisikawaa makwa gii-bimi-aazhawa'adood. Onzaam gipagiigad iwe babagiwayaaniigin gaa-piidooyin. Niwaabowayaan aapiji gipagiigad. Gaawiin gegoo biitoowaabowayaan nindaabajitoosiin. Bezhigwanong dazhibatoo. Bezhigwanong dazhitaa gii-ishpaagonagaanig a'a mooz. Mi go omaa bezhigwanong endazhishimod. Aaniin dash wenji-mawiyan. Geyaabi mawi a'aw biibiiyens. Wegonen wenji-mawiyan. Indaga na'isidoon ginibaaganim. Niwii-na'isidoon i'iw nibaagan. Ningwaagonenan moozonagizh gaa-gii'-ondaabasaman. Gaa-izh-mitanitewang, giga-izhi-nawajiimin; giga-nitiikemin. Ningii-pawaanigoo ji-gigishkamaan zhiibaashka'igani-magoodaas. Awasajiw izhijiwan 'i ziibiins. Awasajiw daa. Ogii-odaapizwaan iniw odewe'iganan -- onzaam jiigaya'ii iwidi ogii-taninaan ishkodeng. Ogii-maanashkinatoon iniwen odaya'iiman imaa gashkibidaaganing. Oowa na' gichi-mamaanitam awe anishinaabewish. Aabitawinaagaans ningii'-minikwen zhoominaabo. Ningii'-mookamanjitoon. Enigok gaandanaamo ikwe wewiib ji-nitaawiginaawasod. Zhaagwenimo ji-gagwedwed ji-anokii'ind. Niwii-gitige ziigwang. Gaye giinawaa o'omaa gitigeg. Aaniin dash apii waa'-maajii-gitigeyan. Mii ganabaj igo ji-aabijibiisaag. Mii 'i  waabang bijiinag ji-gitigeying NImbaapi'idiz gii-waabandamaan biimaakwa'owaan. Dibikong debwewidam gaa-madwe-mawid. Aapiji go agaasitaagozi, maagizhaa abinoojiinh. Giishpin gikendanziwan, gidaa-gagwejimaa gisayenh. Ningii-kagwejimaa nimaamaa aaniin apii ge-bagamibideg i'iw booziwe-odaabaan. Ningii-kagwejimigoo ji-gikinoo'amaageyaan gakinoo'amaadiiyigamigong anishinaabemowin ji-dazhindamaan. Angashkomaa akawe ninga-gagwejimaa. Ogii-maajinizhikawaan iniw bemibatoonid omaa. Gitigewinini omaajinizhikawaa' obizhikiima'. Dibaabam odaabaanag jibwaa-azhebizoyan. Eniwek sa go naa ingii-pi-dibaabamig. Odibaabamaan minik eyaawaad zhooniyaan. Gabe-onaagosh owaazakonendamowaan iniwen nenaa'idaabaanikenid. Gabe-onaagosh inganawaabandaan mezinaateseg. Gichi-michaakozi awe wenda-zhingwaak bedakizod. Bashkwada' mandaaminag. Ningii-onzwaag mandaaminag. Obashkwada'waan iniw omandaaminiman imaa gitigaaning. Aazha apane gii'-awasewa'o. Giishpin minogid ningitigaani-mitig, giga-ondaazhindenaanaan. Gidaa-giboogwaadaan i'iw giboodiyegwaazon. Gichi-agaaming ningii-pi-ondaandawe. Ninaanoondaagomo'aa misawendamaan wii-kaganoonag. "Ambe omaa," indinaa. Aaniin enagindaman manoomin ningo-dibaabiishkoojigan. Agaawaa nin gii-kashkinaa ningozis gii-piibiiyensiwid. Agaawaa ate ziinzibaakwad. Agaawaa go gii-tebise zaasagokwaan. Agaawaa ogashkiwidoon i'iw obimiwanaan a'aw gwiiwizens. Agaawaa gii-te-mizhagaa; gegaa gii-kibozigwaji. Abinoojiinyag agindaasowag bezhig biinish igo ningodwaak. Ngii-waabamaag naanan bakidaabiigishinowaad igiweg zhiishiigwaag imaa michikanaakobijiganing. Minopogozi a'aw adikameg gibozond. Minopogoziwag igiw miskominag. O'owe gidaa-inaaginaa. Ningii-paninaa zhigaagominzh. Anaami-gizhaabikizigan gii-izhi-ditibibizo. Gego wiikaa anooj-igo doodawaaken asemaa. Gego wiikaa gegoo inaaken a'aw inini. Abaabikizwi zhooshkwa'igan Gisinaamagad agwajiing. Gii-izhaayaan, niwiisagigonewe. Gigii'-mooshkinatoon na gimisad. Mooshkinatoon gizhaabikizigan gabe-dibik ji-biskaneg. Ningii'-mooshkinatoon niin ninjiimaan gii-naawakweg. Ambe daga wiisinidaa. Bangii eta go niwiisin. Nindagonaan zhiiwitaagan wiisiniyaan. Endaso-anama'e-giizhigak ko nindawi-wiisinimin iwidi Famous Dave's. Booshke giin wiijiiwiyan oodenaang. Gidaa-wi-wiisinimin imaa wiisiniiwigamigong. Bi-agwaayaandawe gaa-gii-kabaad gaa-bimisemagadinig. Babiiwizhiinyiwag igiw makoonsag gaa-waabamagwaa. Ogii-makamaan iniw oniijaanisan waagaakwad odaminwaagenid. Ogii-naabaakosidoon i'iw waagaakwadosh. Eshkan indawaaj aabajitoodaa. Ingoji apagidoon 'i waagaakwad. Nimaamaa ogii-andawaabamaan iniw wiigobaatigoon. Miish imaa gii-ozhitood iniwen negwaakwaanan. Ayi'ii ogii-aabajitoon iw waagaakwadoons. Waagaakwad aabadad gii-dwaa'igeng, maagizhaa gaye eshkan. Gaa-mamiskojaabid igo a'awe gaa-waabanabid. Wanakwaandag onji-bookobizh waa'-apishimonikaageyan zhingobiig. Gii-wakewizi 'a nabagisag aana-gii-sagaakwa'wag. Atoon imaa nabagisagong. Aandi epa'igod. Naanan ogii-piniweba'waa' binewa' gii-baashkizwaad. Zhiishiibanwii-baashkizigan ogii'-aabajitoon. Odaabajitoonaawaa mekadewaabiigad biiminakwaanens. Gii-teba'oozo na asabaabis imaa gizhaaboniganing. Asabaabisan owii'-adaawenan. Gaa-zhiibizid asabaabisens mazinigwaajigaagen ji-bakisesig zhiibiigishkang omakizinan. Bakam asabaabisens. Aandi ezhinizha'igaadeg. Noomag igo ningii'-naanaagaji'aa enanjiged. Naanaagaji' asin ji-ozhaashaabikizid jibwaa-gabaayan. Gii-ishpi-dagwaagig manoominikaa. Gaa-gigibagiziwaad mitigoog binaakwiiwag gii-ani-ishpi-dagwaagig. Aandi ezhaad. Aandi wendamog? Aandi wenjiiyan. Aandi dash gaa'-onji-noondaman i'iwe. Aandi wendaanimak. Ningikendaan aandi gaa'-atooyan. Aandi enaagoned. Ogii-piimaabika'oodoon zagaabiiginigan gaa-gii'-onji-gashki'od bizhiw. Gii-mamaanjigobinag nindayens booch igo gii-kashki'o. Mii go booch gii-kashki'od awe inday aana-gii-kitaakwapinag. Odoozhiitaa'aan odaanisan waasa waa-tazhi-gikinoo'amawimind. Ozhiitaa'aa' waa'-ando-wanii'igenid. Miinobidoon mazinaakizon gaa-anibegoodeg. Bigwadakamig gidaa-izhiwidoonan ogigishkiganan gaa-gii'-maajaad. "Waasa go apiichaa," gidinendam. Gichi-waasa bimi-debinaagod iwe jiimaan bemi-ayaamagak. Waasa onzaabi. Waasa gii-ina'adoo. Waasa danwewidamoog ma'iinganag. Waasa noopimiing odoondaawanaawaa' asinii' gaa-madoodiswaagewaad. Gego babaamenimaaken. Megwaa odaabaanike. Giga-wanishkwe'aa. Animaasin 'i gimiwanaanakwad omaa gaa-pimi-ayaamagak. Agawaateyaabikaang izhi-agoke aasaakamig. Mii 'imaa wenji-gikendaman aandi nake giiwedinong. Bangii eta go ningii-tagonaan i'iw omb.. ombisijigan gii-bakwezhiganikeyaan. Ginigawinan ombisijigan wii-pakwezhiganikeyan. Gichi-maazhimaate iwe gizhaabikizigan. Awegodogwen dinowa gaa-piindaabikiwebinigaadegwen. Azhiwaasin moozhwaagan giishpin giishkizhaman biiwaabik maagizhaa ge mazina'igan. Giishpin minwa'amaazod apane da-andomaa ji-awi-nagamod. Giishpin dakoosagak ginibewin, giga-zaasaagizideshin. Eniwek igo niminomanji' noongom. Bebesho badakidewan iniw wiigiwaaman. Ishkwe-oodenaang badakide nibewigamig gaa-izhi-nibaayaan Badakide apabiwin jiigishkwaandem. Aandi ezhi-badakideg gimadoodison. Agaamakiing iwidi dazhi-gichi-miigaadim. Anaamisag ko indazhi-gizibiiga'ige giziibiiga'amaan indaya'iiman. Ayaapii ko nimizhodam iwidi izhaayaan endazhi-ataageng. Gii-minwendam gii-pi-ganoonind ji-o-gaagiigidod iwidi endazhi-zagaswe'iding. Agwanaateng dazhi-anwebidaa. Niboodaakwen iwe bigishkiboode-wiiyaas wii-naboobiikeyaan. Gabaatoon 'i wiiyaas. Obi-zaagidoomaan ogwizisensan. Dikinaaganing dakobizowan. Niwii-o-biinjwebinige iwidi mazina'iganiiwigamigong. Gigagiibaadendaagoz. Gagwe-minjiminan iwe gaa-izhi-onagimigooyin imaa gii-piinjwebinigeng. Mii igo ezhi-niiskikaad 'aw animosh miginaad ini makwan. Gii-pagamaajimaa gii-miikoshkoozod awe zhimaaganish iwidi endazhiikodaading, Indaga gabaawebishkan ini mitigoonsan imaa aawadaasoowidaabaanensing. Ogii-wiiyagitoon gii-adaawaaged odaawadaasoowidaabaanens. Mino-maajiiginoon ningitigaanan. Gichi-neniibowa odaabajitoon 'i wiisagad 'a jiibaakwewinini jiibaakwed. Anooj igo apa'idiwag igiw abinoojiinyag gaa-kaazootaadiwaad. Awasikana imaa bimademo awe abinoojiinh. Indaga nawadin awe abinoojiinh; onzaam jiigaya'ii imaa ayaa bagizowining. Babaaminizhikodaadiwag igiweg abinoonjiiyag bepeshinidiwaad. Agwajiing odaminowag abinoojiinyag. Ogii-kwiinawendaan 'iw gaa-andawendang gaa-onji-mindawed. Wegonen endawendaman ji-biidaamawinaan. Gidaa-ningaagonasige nibi andawendaman. Aasamaatig badakide i'iwe endawaabandaman. Giishpin dakozigwaag gigiziibiiga'igan, gii-giziibiigiiyan giga-babiishigonaan. Gii-aazhawibizo imaa eshpaanig aazhogan. Bekaa bimibizon aazhawibizowin zaaga'igan gaa-gikendanziwan. Maagizhaa gidaa-bitaabikishin Na' gichi-wawiyazhinaagozi awe ikwezens -- indigo naa go aw odaminwaagan. Ogii'-agaashiinyi'aan gaa-gii'-ozhitamawaad odaminwaaganensan odaanisensan. Wegonen neboobiikaadang. Ozhiitaawag igiw mewine'igewaad. Mii azhigwa makadekewaad. Mii iwidi debinaagozid ogidaaki wa'aw gaa-ni-maajaad. Ogidaaki awi-dazhi-wiisinidaa. Ogidaaki iwidi ingii-pabaa-ayizhaa. Niizhwaabik ashi-aabita odinagimaan iniwen midaaso-dibaabiishkoojigan iniw opiniin. Ogii-sagaswe'aan iniw owiijikiwenyan ji-giizhaakonamowaad iw obabaamiziwiniwaa. Onzaam gabaya'ii ogii-mazina'amaagoon gaa-onji-naadazina'iged. Aaniin ezhimaasod. Oboogizikaagon iwe miskojiisiminaaboo. Gagwe-minotoon iwe zhiiwaagamizigan wezhitooyin. Ambe niimiitamawaadaa gaa-oshki-biindigeshimod. Waabigwaniinsan ngii-naabakiinaanan. Niwii-kagwe-nitaawigitoonan. Gaawiin ganabaj indaa-debwetawaasii gaa-gii-kagwejimid wii'-wiidigemid. Bekaa niwii-ozhibii'ige jibwaa-maajaaying. Miiwa' owe oniijaanisa'. Ginoozi aw oshki-inini. Aaniin ekoozid gigozis. Ishkwaaj gii-waabamag, aazha ani-ginooziiban. Giinawaa weshkinaweyiyeg apane gidaa-wiiji'aawaa gichi-anishinaabe. Ogii-maadanokaadaan gaa-inanoonind awasonaago. Awasonaago ningii-izhaa gichi-oodenaang. Ingii-koshkomaa awe nimishoomis gii-piibaagimag awe abinoonjii. Niwii-pagwa'aan niwaabowayaan gaa-biigoshkaag. Bedowe gaagiigidod a'awe inini. Mii iniw gaa-andawenimaad ji-bi-gaagiigidonid gaa-onji-andomaad. Miigwechiwi' awe gaa-gaagiigidod. Biinji-dewe'igan gaagiigido manidoo. Ningiiniboodoon i'iw mookomaan Niwii-kiiniboodoon nimookomaan jibwaa-maajii-bakonigeyaan. Nabagi-zisiboojigan aabajitoon giiniboodoooyan gimookomaan. Onzaam gagaanwaawan iniwen bawa'iganaatigoon. Naanaagaji' asin ji-ozhaashaabikizid jibwaa-gabaayan. Gii'-ani-mikawi. Ani-aabiziishin. Gii'-aabiziishin. Niizho-diba'igan eta gii'-nibo. Oshki-aya'ii ogii-piidoon. Giga-zhooshkwaabooz giishpin dakokaadaman baatebagoon. Anang gii-piidagoojin. Bagakaasigewag anangoog. Ayaangwaamizin. Gego ozhaashishingen. Ingii-padakininjiishin imaa migiskaning. Aaniin waa'-inigokotood waakaa'igan gaa-wii'-ozhitood. Baamaa gii'-ningagwindeg doodooshaabo, giga-gigizhebaa-wiisinimin. Ezhi-wiinijaaned 'a gwiiwizens ezhi-inind ji-ziiniskiigomed. Zhebaa ningii-awi-waabamaa ozhibii'igewikwe. Niwii'-wiiji'ig gaa-gii-kagwedweyaan. Onzaam wiiba ningii'-amaji'igoo zhebaa. Gigizheb ngii'amaji'ig 'a noozhishenh. Nibwaanawi'aa ji-giishkowed awe aabidademod. Biminizha'an imaa ezising mazina'iganing. Aaniin wenji-wiiweginaman iniw mazina'iganan. Azhiwaasin moozhwaagan giishpin giishkizhaman biiwaabik maagizhaa ge mazina'igan. Onjida ogii-moo'aan iniwen oshiimenyan. Giishpin apane miikindizid da-moo'aa wiiba. Gego miigaanaaken gijiimens. Giga-moo'aa. Dabasaakosin aazhogan Gichi-mookomaanakiing gaa-izhi-aazhawamog. Zhaaganaashiiwakiing onji-maadamon. Odaabaanaak aabadizi gegoo gii-naajidaabiing. Miskwaabiigad 'i biiminakwaanens. Gidaa-wiisookawaag apane gichi-anishinaabeg. Gegoo imaa giga-onji-gikendaan ge-ani-izhi-mino-bimaadiziyan. Nimbizindawaag igiweg niizhoodenyag geganoonidiwaad. Wiiji-odaminoondiwag niizhoodenyag. Niwanitoonan ndaabaabika'iganan. Anaamaabikong atewan iniw aabaabika'iganan. Gaadamaw gidaabaabika'iganan. Gaawiin mashi omazina'iganisii ji-bimibizod. Gii'-wani-gaadamaazo odaabaabika'iganan. Gaawiin omikanziinan. Biiwaabiko-giishkiboojiganens gidaa-aabajitoon ji-bookwaabikiboonad gashkaabika'igan giishpin gii-wanitooyan gidaabaabika'igan. Aapiji biichaa onigam gaa-gii'-izhi-gabadoowaang; aabitoonigam ningii'-ani-bagijinige. Awegonen o'owe? Inashke goda waabandan o'owe. Aaniish ge-izhichigaadamaan o'owe ji-anokiimagak. Gii-ozisin zhigwa iwe ge-izhichigeng o'owe dibaakonigewin. O'owe na, maagizhaa ge mii owe. O'owe na, maagizhaa ge owe. Mii imaa godagiing wenjiwidaasod awe gemoodaatigwed Nawaj mashkawapidoon gidadimanan. Wewiib aabiskobidoon gidadiman. Debinaagwad 'iw Ogaakaaning iwidi agaaming. "Waasa go apiichaa," gidinendam. Aaniin epiichaag oodenaang? |  Niisimidana daso-diba'igan apiichaa. Aaniin epiichaag ezhi-wekwaamog miikana. Nagaakamii awe inday aana-maajinizha'wag. Mii go iwidi gaa-ina'adooyaan dibikong gii-izhaayaan. Mii go naasaab ena'adood iniwen bema'anaad. Booch igo ingii-kashkitoon aana-gii-gichi-zanagak owe gaa-inanoonigooyaan. Zanagadini enwed 'a gaagiigidod. Gawiin ninisidotawaasii. Gii-kabenaage ge-zhooniyaansiwataaged. Gii-ziigwang agwaataawag miskwaadesiwag gii-ando-owaawanowaad. Gegaa ningii-pisikawaa makwa gii-bimi-aazhawa'adood. Ningii-tazhwaanikweyaabaawe gii-ani-aazhawa'adoowaan jibwaa-biindigawag nindaanis. Ombweyaagama'an ginaboobiim jibwaa-agwaabikideg. Awanjish ogii-maandandaan iwe dekaag aana-dewaabided. Gii-aabijibizowag igiweg zhigaagong gaa-izhaawaad. Endaso-gigizheb ko nizaagidinaa ninday. Endaso-gigizheb agwajiing ninando-biindaakoojige. Aaniin epiitowed. Gaawiin de-apiitowesii ge-nisidotawagiban. Ninga-jiishada'aan akwaandawaagan. Jiishada'igan aabajitoon ji-jiishada'aman gaa-gii-pinizaman. Oziinziningwaandaan bimiwidood. Weweni obimiwidoon odizhinikaazowin. Zhaabonigan obimiwidoon waabizheshi. Anooj igo gegoo nimegadeshkaagon zhakamoyaan. Indaga minjiminan o'ow bikwaakwad. Gigagiibaadendaagoz. Gagwe-minjiminan iwe gaa-izhi-onagimigooyin imaa gii-piinjwebinigeng. Daga maajaan miinawaa nagamon. Gigagwaanisagitaagoz gosha. Gaye niin ningii-noonde-nibaa. Gaye niin ingii-wiiji'iwe. Ogii'-miikinzomaan wiitaawisan gii-waabamaad. Megwayaak ingii-pabaa-ayizhaa. Onzaam gichi-michaabiigad 'i biiminakwaan. Gaawiin gidaa-aabajitoosiimin. Biinichigewag imaa eyedawikana. Ningii-kwanabaabog gii-bi-niishiboonoyaan. Obimoondaan i'iw manoomin. Ogii-mikwaasenodawaawaan iniw makwan iwidi gii-inaatewebinigewaad. Debweweboojigewag giishka'aakwewinini. Oganawaabandaan i'iw ziibi bimijiwaninig. Wewayiiba miigaadiwag igi abinoojiinyag. Wewayiiba ndamajise. Gii-bitikonidizo awe wezhikodangiban iwe okij gaa-onji-giizhikawaasig ini opwaaganan. Ingii-anookii ji-izhiwijigaadeg injiimaan ji-dazhiikigaadeg. Ambegish mino-giizhigak waabang. Gidaa-andobinewemin. Gichiwishkaa giwanii'igan. Noopiming ingii-izhaa gii-kiiyoseyaan. Oshkiniigikweg iwidi mawinzowag noopiming. Gichi-zakide noopiming. Gego iwidi izhaaken. Bangii nindewaawigane. Omaamiginaan iniw odoopiniiman. Oziiginaan imaa gichi-onaaganing. Mii imaa gaa-tazhi-nase'ang i'iwe gii-ozhitood ziinzibaakwad. Niwii-kiziibiigizide jibwaa-agonjidooyaan inzidan imaa gichi-onaaganing. Nindagazomig gii-dibaajimod endasobiboonweyaan. Mii aazha gii'-oditang de-dasobiboonwed ji-ishkwaa-anokiid. Atoon imaa jiibaakwewakikong. Gichi-mindido aw jiibaakwewakik. Ogichi-aabiinzomaan iniw onaabeman aw ikwe gii-o-jaagaaboojigenid. Gaawiin igo anishaa gii-izhichigesii. Gegoo go gii-ondizi imaa. Bangii eta ningii'-ondiz gaa-gii'-inanokii'igoowaan. Ayaangwaamizin. Aapiji ozhaashikwaa iwidi ezhaayin. Gii-ayaangwaamizi ji-gwayakozhang i'iw gaa-anoonind ji-giishkizhang. Ayaangwaamiziwag wii-kabenaadiwaad. Ogii-sagaswe'aan iniw owiijikiwenyan ji-giizhaakonamowaad iw obabaamiziwiniwaa. Mashkawegad miinawaa gagwaanisaginigwad iwe badagwana'igan. Mii 'iw gii-odaapideg iwe badagwana'igan. Gii-waabananokii awe gabe-dibik gaa-ondendid. Ingii-oshki-biindige imaa anaam... anama'ewigamigong. Mii imaa gii-waabangeyaan ojijiingwanabing anami'aang. Aakoziiyigamigong dapine. Miikawaadizi a'aw ogimaakwe gaa-waabamag. Nibwaanawiwidoonan aana-wii-aawadooyaan iniw misan. Ogii-gichi-wiisagipwaan iniwen zhingaangawinzhiin gaa-bakwemaad. Gichi-maazhichige naa awe gaa-pi-bakwemaad iniwen aasamaakwa'iganan. Ge niinawind ningii'-aanikanootaamin ikidowinan. Ogii-mashkawi'aan iniw mazinichiganan gaa-... gaa-ozhikonaad. Giishpin besho-giizhigak, wiiba giga-nibaamin. Aabita-biboon aapiji besho-giizhigad. Gii-kwayakogiizhwe gii-tibaajimod iwe gaa-izhwebadinig. Ogii-mashkawisidoon gii-tibaajimod 'iw gaa-izhiwebadinig. Aanind ogaadoon enaajimod. Gaawiin gakina dibaajimosii. Giishpin noondawad diindiisi noondaagozid gii-biboong, dibaajimo noomag wii'-aabawaanig. Odenaniw obiijimaanjigaagen; mii ezhichiged ginebig. Aazha gikendaagozi awenen ge-niiwezhiwed niigaanendaagoziwin. Gaawiin niminwendanziin gaa-wiisagang. Aapiji minopogwad oshki-manoomin, wakewide gaye. Miigwechiwi' awe gaa-gaagiigidod. Maajaan ishke naa owi-miigwechiwi' awe. Onzaam bangii ningii'-miigwechiwi'aa. Omayaawishimaan odakikoon jibwaa-ziigaagonashinid. Mashkikii-adaawewigamigong ogii-ondinaan i'iw ozosodamoo-mashkiki. Aandi gaa-ondinaman giwewebanaabaan. | Adaawewigamigong ingii-ondinaan. Giga-waabamin apii ojiindiwi-giizhigak. Minjinawezi 'aw abinoonjiiyens dekaanig. Gii-minjinawezi gii-niiwenimind ini zhooshkwaada'enid aana-gii-ataagewaad. Bangii ogii-minikwen 'iw doodooshaaboo. Doodooshaaboo imaa ningii-atoon dakisijiganing. Ogii-bichi-ziigwebinaan doodooshaaboo. Twaayaa gii-maazhisin iwe doodooshaaboo. Ingii-minikwen bangii. Gichi-wiinate 'iw waakaa'igan. Ishkweyaang iwidi waakaa'iganing atewan ini misan. Giiwedin. Wiikwaasin wii-kisinaag. Wiikwaasinjigan aabajitoon wii-chiishada'igeyan. Wiikwaasinoon gaa-biiwisingin michisag. Giishpin ditisadowed gidamikwayaan, gaawiin aapiji daa-aginzosii. Giishpin nisad waawaashkeshi gaa-agaashiinyid, da-nookiiwagizi. Da-nookiiwagad wiiyaas. Ogii-paaswaan iniw omashwen gaa-onji-niimagoonaad. Aaboojiigin gii-paaswad nigigwayaan. Awegwen igo odaa-noondawaan aandi eyaanid ininishiban gaa-initaagozid. Ingii-pawaadaan babaamaashiyaan giizhigong. Ogii-tibaadodaan i'iw gaa-pawaadang gii-minwaabandang 'iw gichi-niimi'idiwin. Niizho-mininj gii'-maajiigi noongom gaa-biboong noozhis Dana. Ningii-siikoobiigamaa bagesaan. Agwaashim giigoonyag gii-ishkwaa-naadasabiiyan. Niizhoonikenin wii'-agwaashimad gijiibaakwaanakik. Gizhaabikizo. Anaamakamig dazhigiwag bagaanag. Nindaanis ogii-tagozwaan bagaanan gii-ozhi'aad bakwezhiganan. Akawe niwii-pinaakwe'odiz jibwaa-maa'ishkamaan. Ishkwaa-niso-diba'iganeg da-booniiwag igiw gaa-maa'ishkamowaad. Gii-ziigwang agwaataawag miskwaadesiwag gii-ando-owaawanowaad. Miskwaadesi zaagikwegomo naawi-ziibi. Gii-odaapinigaazo awe miigis omaa gaa-pimi-abid. Jiigi-waakaa'igan dana'amaazo. Aandi nanda endana'amaazod gaa-debwewidang. Aaniin epiitizid gidaanis. Mii go eyiizh epiitiziwaad. Zhaagooj igo inendam wii'-izhichiged. Aangwaamas iidog mii gii-kiizhitooyaan nimaawandoogwaasonikaan. Wewiib gagwe-giizhitoon gaa-dazhiikaman gigikinoo'amaagoowin. John ogii-kiizhitoon jiimaan gaa-gii'-ozhitood. Onzaam mangadezi a'aw nabagisag gaa-piinad. Giwii'-awi-ganawaabamaag ina giin gaa-wii-kagwejiiwaanidiwaad noongom gaa-dibikak. Aaniin apii waa'-oshkidaabaaneyan? Gichi-zaasaakwe awe mindimooyenh epiichi-jiikimigod iniw dewe'iganan miinawaa negamonid. Waa, giinetawind gigii-saasaakwemin. Gii-piniwebaasin waabowaan gaa-gii'-adoodooyaan ji-baateg. Gii-piniwebaasin gaagaagiwi-wazison. Ogii-kagwejichige'aan iniwen odayan ji-nitaa-odaabiinid. Gabaya'ii ondendiwag igiweg naadaabowewaad. Mii go wenda-zhigajibii'indwaa. Mii imaa oshki-noogishkaawigamigong gii-pi-noogishkaad awe gaa-shigajibii'ag bijiinaago. Obookosidoon waagaakwad gii-dwaa'iged; onzaam gipagadin. Gii-mashkawisin gaa-izhibii'iged a'aw odaake-ogimaa. Mashkawisin gaa-ototoseg. Mazinaagoneshin gaa'-izhi-nibaad waawaashkeshi. Niineta ingii-izhaa zagaswe'iding. Ogii-pabaa-ikwapinaan iniwen asabiin bijiinag miinawaa ..niswanama'e-giizhikwagak da-bagida'waam. Gii-oshki-niibing apii bakwaniiwan wiigwaasan. Mishawikwam awi-bagidaabiin. Mishawikwam dazhi-wewebanaabii. Wenda-ojaanimitaawaad igi esigibii'igewaad. Gii-paashkikaamagadini imaa gii-miniiwizided. Ogii-kiizhiikaanan gii-ozhikodang iniw abwiin. Ambe shke o-mazinaatesijigedaa iwidi mazinaatesijigewigamigong. Aamoo-ziinzibaakwad nindagonaan imaa nitiing. Ayaangodino ko bi-dagoshin indinawemagan bimi-mawadishid. Niwii-o-mawadisaag igiw agaamiiwininiwag awaswaabang. Gabe-giizhig nimawadisaanaan Anangokwe. Ningii'-awi-mawadisaa nookomis zhebaa. Wiinge go ani-oziigiingwe. Gichi-aya'aawi. Aana-gii-niigaanii awe giigidoowinini gaa-bakinawind. Biindoonag abiwag igiw asabiig. Aayaanikoobiwag midaaso ingiw indasabiig. Anaamikwam bimi-inabi a'aw asab. Gidaa-bakinaa gidasab ji-baaswad. Onaazibiiwinaan odasabiin waa'-ando-bagida'waad. Aaboojiigin gii-paaswad nigigwayaan. Biiniigad ina gidadoopowiniigin. Nabagisag apishim gijiibaakwaanakik ji-jaagidesinog gidadoopowiniigin. Midaaso-diba'igaans gii-izhise. Gaawiin igo aapiji inzaazaabiisii. Mii zhigwa adimigooyaan awe gikaawin. Wegonen gaa-kiishkizhigaageyan gii-giishkizhaman bashkwegin. Ingodwewaan indaa-gii-adaawenan ini waawanoon. Baakinamaan mi... gii-midaachinoon eta go. Giiwedinong ondaanimad wenji-gisinaag. Gisinaamagad agwajiing. Wiiwindibepizon. Gii-kashkadin i'iw zaaga'igan gii-kisinaag. Gichi-gisinaadog igo. Bakwenaamowag igiweg mishtadimoog. Wii-gichi-gisinaamagad waabang. Anangoog bagakaanzhewag; noomag igo wii-kisinaa. Biida'amaazo nookomis biidaasamosed. Ogii-mawinanaawaan gii-nakweshkawaawaad iniw baadaasamosenid. Niinitamawind iidog inga-onzaamin ziinzibaakwadaaboo. Niinitamawind ngii-kagagwejimigoomin. Zhaagawibagizi miskwaabiimagoons. Mii awe miskwaabiimagoons ge-aabaji'ad ge-waakaagwa'wad gibiskitenaaganikaaning. "Onzaamiinad iidog i'iwe manoomin imaa Manoomini-ziibiing," mii 'i gaa-ikidod ni... nimisenh. Onzaamiinadoon miinan omaa zhingwaakokaang. Indaga biindigadoon apishimonan. Nindatoon iwe apishimon imaa n... michisag wii-nibaayaan. Maamaagojiishkan boodaajii'igan wii-poodaajii'aman gidapishimon. Gii-ogimaawi'aa awe indoozhim omaa epiitakamigak aabita-niibing. Indayaawaanaan awe dinowa gaazhagens gaa-biigwawed. Giigoonyag, zhiishiibag indizhi-mashkawaakwajimaag nimashkawaakwajiji-makakong. Ingii-mamoon 'iw baashkizigan imaa gaa-ateg. Endaso-giizhik iko nimamoonan nimashkikiinsiman. Onaabandan weweni iwe waa-mamooyan. Aanak nanagamo ge-ani-onaagoshig. Aanawenjigaazowan obakwezhiganikaanan; onzaam aakwaakadozowan, gaye bibagiziwan Gii-wenipazhise gaa-inanoonigooyaan ji-asigisidooyaan. Gakina awiya oodenaang izhaawag. Gakina awiya gidaa-manaaji'aa. Mii iwidi gaa-o-dazhi-agoodood, jiigashkosiw. Waasaakwanjigewag waaboozoog. Mii omaa ge-izhi-agoodooyang. Gete-anishinaabeg wiidoopandiwag. Weweni inanjige'idizon. Gego miijiken gaa-boozaag. Mii go aanawi gii-ombishkaad awe bakwezhigan gaa-onadinag. Gichi-weweni ikwanaamo awe nimishoomis gaa-pi-zaaga'ang. Awasaatig iwidi gii-izhaa gii-o-zaaga'ang. Gaag obishagaakwamaa' mitigoo'. Ingii-kanoonaa ondaas imaa ji-bi-inabid. Anaamikwam bimi-inabi a'aw asab. Mikwamiiwan miikana. Ozhaashamon. Bekaa daga bii'ishin. Bekaa niwii-chiibaakwe. Bekaa niwii-ozhibii'ige jibwaa-maajaaying. Bekaa. Akawe niwii-ozhiiginige. Nimanepwaa. Bekaa. Bii'aadaa awe. Nawaj bekaa ikidon. Bekaa akawe. Bekaa kawe. Jiigi-gizhaabikizigan onji-baasan gidazhiganan. Mii go imaa ezhi-wiikoshkaawaad zakaatenig igiw waa-abizowaad. Mii imaa godagiing wenjiwidaasod awe gemoodaatigwed Mii 'iw gii-ogichidaawid inaadizookaanaa awe gaa-panendaagozid. Aaniin enaateseg. Bi-zaagidademo gaa'-ishkwaa-ganawaabandang enaatesenig. Nisawaabik ningii'-waabamaa ginebig. Gegaa gii-kawajiwag igi animoonsag gaa-izhi-biindiganagwaa. Niwawiyadenimaa awe animoons ezhinaagozid. Maanaadizi. Mii 'i zhigwa gii-pakwaabiwaad igiweg animoonsag. Mizhisha iwidi debinaagwad aana-gii-inag ji-o-gaadood 'iw odoodaabaan. Onandoojiinaan 'iw biskanebijigaans.  | Ogii-mikoojiinaan ina? Apane naa ani-bishkotaagwad iwe ishkodewidaabaan omaa gaa-pimibidemagak. Mii 'iw gii-oniijaanisid awe gidayinaan. Zhaangaso gii-ayaaw...  ogii-ayaawaan iniw animoonsan. Gego babaamenimaaken igiweg animoonsag. Aapiji gizhaawaso awe weniijaanisid. Adisan giinizisan. Aandi enaawanaad asinii'. Ogii-gipagikonaan iniwen zhiiwitaagani-gookooshan dezhiikawaad. Manginaagozi mikwam gaa-waasishing minisaabikong. Gichi-gezika gwekibide iwe bemiseg ishpiming. Giishpin ozhaawishkwakoneg ishkode gii-biboong wii'-aabawaa. Naawi-baawitig inaaboono gaa-niishiboonod. Biite gizhibaayaaboode naawi-baawitig. Niinawind iko nimaamaayiban ngii-chiiga'amegwemin. Aaniin epiitagoojing. Badakakiise mookomaan gii-apagidooyaan. Gegoo wii'-minose. Onzaam wayiiba gii-kijigwaashkwani imaa manoominike-jiimaanensing gaa-onji-gwanabisenig. Ogii-naada'oodoon iwe manoominike-jiimaanens gaa-maadaasininig. Aana-onji'agwaa igiw abinoojiinyag, onjida miigaadiwaad. Bemijigamaag indaana-gii-izhaa andawanokiiyaan. Nibwaanawinaa 'aw ditibidaabaanens aana-wii-ombinag. Ogigishkaan nibabiinzikawaagan aana-wii-piizikamaan. Aana-wii-koji'aa ji-anokaadang. Nindaana-gii-kagwejimaa ji-manisawid. Gaawiin idash mashi. Andoojiishkan akawe miikana jibwaa-aazhawagaakobizoyan. Indaabajitoon abwewinaabik zaasagokwaanag a'aw bakwezhigan. Ozaasagokwaanaan iniw opiniin awe nookomis. Niwii-saasagokwaanaa giikanaamozigan. Miiwan onowe. Ondaasikana maa gii-pakebizo. Giga-wanishin giishpin banitawad imaa ge-onji-bakebizoyan. Gii-pinigwaashkoni jibwaa-bakebizod. Mii awe ge-biinjwebinigetamowindiban menogaabawid omaa ayaaying. Gaawiin igo minogaabawisii 'aw ogichidaa; onzaam zhaagode'e. Boonitoon iwe. Gego babaamendangen. Dabasaanakwadook oboonitoon ataagewin. Boonitoon apane nebaajiikaman minikwewinish. Niwii-poonitoon minikweyaan ow zhingobaaboo. Nimbaninaan iwe onaagaans ezhi-biigosing. Ogii-andoojiishkaan 'iw ozhooniyaa-mashkimodens gaa-paninang imaa gashkii-dibikatenig ji-... odaabaaniiwigamigong. Ogii-paashkisidoon iniw waawanoon gaa-paninang. Gii-panaandawe gaa-niisaaboojiged. Ozaawaagamin makade-mashkikiwaabo. Ozaawadaawangad makade-mashkikiwaabo. Giimooj gii-ni-giimii a'aw nindaanis. Giimooj igo niwii-wiindamawaa 'a mindimooyenh. Giimooj ogaganoonaan. Giimooj oodenaang niwii-izhaa. Ojaanimakamigiziwag igiweg wezhiitaawaad. Makadewikonayen owii-pi-waabamigowaan. Waakaa'igewininiwag gekinoo'amawindwaa ezhigiizhwewaad "ninitaawichigemin". Dakaabikishin nindoodaabaan. Gaawiin maajiibizosii. Akawe ningii'-asemaake jibwaa-bi-maajiibizowaan endaayaan. Mino-gaashaa ningiishkiboojigan. Gaawiin gaashaasinoon nimoozhwaagan.
