Mamigoshkan manoomin ji-gidashkishkaman. Gabedibik giiwana'amaazo. Iwidi ogii-odaabaadaan awasisag i'iwe gashkibidaagan. Gii-bapagoshkaa i'iw makizin gaa-bapagwa'ang. Naanan ogaawan ogii-ishkonaan. Ogii-onagimaan iniw naanan ininiwan gaa-anoonaad. Ogii-madaabiiwinaan iniwen naanan odasabiin. Aandi enwewebiisaag. Gii-pangishin babaamaandawed awe abinoonjiinh. Ogii-pagijwebinaan iwe omitigwaab gii-tabazi'aad ini mitigoon bengishininid. Ningii-pangishin gaa-izhi-wiisagidooskwaneyaan. Anooj igo ina'amaazo, apagamod ini aadizookaanan. Baamaa ningizod amik, ninga-gabaashimaa. Mii 'i gii-mookibidood i'iw odasanjigowin awe zazaagiz. Mii miinawaa ji-niimi'iding iwidi gaa-waabaabiganikaang aabitawangizod awe ode'imini-giizis. Nookomis madwe-biibaagi agaaming. Omagakii apii gii-biibaagid, mii 'i zhigwa wii'-aamiwad namewag. Naada'wik agaaming gaa-madwe-biibaagid. Wanakwaandag onji-bookobizh waa'-apishimonikaageyan zhingobiig. Bijiinag gigizheb inga-ozhi'aa a'aw bakwezhigan. Gigizheb ningii-onishkaa gii-piindaakoojigeyaan. Gii-naniizaanidizo a'aw gaa-odaminwaaged iwe eshkan. Gichi-weweni ikwanaamo awe nimishoomis gaa-pi-zaaga'ang. Giishpin wawaabishe'od giizhigo-giizis, wii-kisinaa. Gichi-mooseg indayaawaag. Gidayaawaa na asemaa. Imbaas. Indayaawaanaan awe gaazhagens dinowa gaa-biigwawed. Gii-paashkine-biiwan. Gaawiin ganage debinaagwasinoon agaami-zaaga’igan. Bijiinaago ningii-kinisinaa'ogomin agaami-zaaga'igan onzaam gii'-mamaangaashkaa. Mii iw gii-maajiikigaadeg i'iw miikana waa-nanaa'ichigaadeg. Bijiinaago ingii-pi-wanibiz gii-bi-dagoshinaan omaa. Nanaa'ichigaade miikana. Gagwaanisa minwaabadad iwe biimaskwaakwa'igan imaa wekoshinowaad igi mitigoog. Giiwedaabaazh amik gaa-gii-tasoonad. Ningiiwedaabaanigoo. Ganabaj ningii-pookogaadeshin. Gego imaa izhi-gabaaken. Nibiiwaabikaa. Giga-ozhaashaabikishin. Ogiji-adoopowin gii-pimaandawewag ingiw abinoojiinyag. Anaamidaabaan zhingishin animoonzhish. Gaawiin wiiyaas ninitaa-miijisiin. Gii-nookide i'iw wiiyaas. Agokadoon 'i wiiyaas imaa abwaanaakong. Weweni ogii-webizhaan 'i wiinin imaa wiiyaasing. Niwii'-mashkawaakwajidoon wiiyaas gaa-gii'-miinigooyaan. Nindoodita'aan waa'-izhi-gabeshiyaan. Jiigidaabaan namadabi nimaamaa. Ganabaj awiya obaabii'aan. Mizhishawaya'ii danakamigiziwag igi zhaawanoowininiwag beshkwada'igewaad. Odabizwaa' ominjikaawanini jibwaa-biizikamoonaad oniijaanisan. Gipagizi aw mikwam imaa zaaga'iganing. "Ondaashaan omaa bi-izhaan," nindig nookomis. Gego gigigwaashkoniken gibaashkizigan. Maagizhaa awiya gidaa-bichinawaa. Ogii-onaakonaan a'aw dibaakonigewinini iniw gimoojishkiiwininiwan. Ganabaj aanjigondaagane awe wenji-maanitaagozid. Gii-makadewaaso; onzaam gabaya'ii gii-ayaa iwidi aasamaatenig. Giziibweweshkaa awe ditibidaabaanens: onzaam agwaagwaabikishin. Makadewiingwe a'awe gechi-wiinaanagiingwed. Wiinaanagiingwe 'a ikwezens izhaad oodenaang. Owiijiiwaan omaamaayan. Giga-wiiji-giiyosemin. Mooz giga-andawaabamaanaan Ingoji go niizho-diba'igan ingii-tanakamigizimin gii-andawaabamangid gaa-wanishing awe abinoojiinyens. Andawaabam egaasibagizid. Ogidaaki iwidi debinaagozi a'awe endawaabamad. Onandawaabamaan iniw gaa-maakinawaad waawaashkeshiwan. Ginoondesemin makade-mashkikiwaabo. Andawaabamaadaa Timii. Naaning ningii-madaabii gii-andawaabamagwaa igiw abinoojiinyag. Andawaabam gizhooniyaa jibwaa-giba'igaadeg zhooniyaawigamig. Ahaaw akawe nindasemaa ninga-andawaabamaa. Ningii-mikawaamaa ningozis ji-adaawed bakwezhiganan. Gidaa-mikawaamaa ezhi-anishinaabewinikaazod. Gidaa-bakinaa gidasab ji-baaswad. Aaboojiigin gii-paaswad nigigwayaan. Zhiibaabizon gaa-izhi-zhiibaajiwang. Niizh niwii-kabaashimaag ininishibag. Bedaajiwanzwaanakik niwii'-aabaji'aa. Geget nindebwetaan nindinaabandamowin. Gaa-izhi-miigaadiwaad igiw niizh abinoojiinyag, mii dash awe gikinoo'amaagewikwe ogii-kaganoonaan. Ajina go ningii-kaganoonaa jibwaa-boozid gichi-odaabaanan. Ningii-kaganoonaag igiweg weshki-bimaadiziwaad weshki-maadanokiiwaad. Nimiinaa a'a abinoojiinh bakwezhigaansan. Ogii-chekibiinaan obakwezhigaansiman ji-nookaabaawenid. Gii-pakwadaasinoon iniwen aniibiishan omaa gii-gichi-nooding awasonaago. Gizhiibani'o oshkiniigikwe agwinaanan gaa-agwiid. Onitaa-ozhi'aan opwaaganan. Ingoding ngo-giizhik eta go dazhitaa ji-giizhi'aad. Gichi-weweni ingii-piini'aa indoopwaagan. Ona'ishimaan odoopwaaganan imaa ebinid. Niwii-mooshkina'aa nindoopwaagan. Ishpimiing odinoo'igaagenan odoopwaaganan gaa-gaagiigidod. Gii-manezi gaa-onji-andodamaaged iwe ashandiwin. Aandi endanwewenjiged amik? | Agaami-zaaga'igan danwewenjige. Anaamoonag iko ningii-tazhi-odaminomin. Naawi-zaaga'igan iko ningii-pagidawaamin. Aaniin epiichiid gaa-anokaadang waakaa'igan. Zhigwa na odapakwaadaan. Omegwaa-ningizaan 'i wiinin a'aw mindimooyenh. Niwii'-ningizaan wiiyaas jibwaa-gabaatoowaan. Ningizan ashkikomaan. Wiimbikozh nabagisag. Mii 'imaa izhi-ziiginan gaa-gii'-ningizaman ashkikomaan. Dabasa'amoog we'weg. Wiiba wii-soogipon. Gichi-bagakaasige awe dibiki-giizis aana-aabitawaabikizid. Agaamakiing iwidi dazhi-gichi-miigaadim. Gichi-wawiingezi gikinootawaad ini migiziin awe ogichidaa. Naniizaanendam ji-ipizonikepan imaa gichi-oodenaang. Andawaabandan i'iw gichi-gwaaba'igan. Gichi-waasa bimi-debinaagod iwe jiimaan bemi-ayaamagak. Gichi-mewinzha gii-izhaayaambaan oodenaang. Gichi-weweni ingii-piini'aa indoopwaagan. Gewiinawaa na gii'-ayaawag iwidi gaa-gii-tazhi-zagaswe'iding. Aaniish enigokwaakwak Ogii-noominaan 'i abwewin wii-saasagokwed. Bigishkishin 'aw diba'igeziswaanens gaa-pangishing. Mookwamandam gaa-nitaawiginaawasod. Mii 'iw aangwaamas gii-odisidiwaad igiweg niizhoodenyag. Mii aangwaamas gii-apaginaad ini gichi-gwiiwizensan gegwaajiiwaanaad. Aangwaamas gii-te-nibaayaan. Aangwaamas iidog mii gii-kiizhitooyaan nimaawandoogwaasonikaan. Gashkiiwaanakwad noongom. Mii 'iw aangwaamas zaagaasiged 'aw giizis. Ingii-wanitawaa awe gaa-kaagiigidod aninishibag gii-tazhimaad. Biinji-wiish danwewegamitoo amik. Mii iwe wayeshkad gaa-izhichigewaad mewinzha gii-... gii-onakidoowaad waaginogaan. Giminjimenimaa na gii'-megwaashkawadiban wa'awe. Anaamidaabaaning zhegoshin nanaa'idaabaaned. Nimaamaa ko ogii-nookizwaan iniw esibanan. Gokeyawikaadan giwanii'igan. Nawaj igo obiimendaan 'iw gaa-inaakonind gii-... gii-tibaakonind. O-gikinjigwen awe gigete-gwiiwizensim. Ambe daga wiisinidaa. Daga miizhishin zhooniyaa. Gizibiiga'an daga iwe waabishkiigin. Wiinad. Daga ininamawishin 'i dekonaman. Mii gii-kiizhideg gii-naboobiikeyaan. Ogii-tawisidoon ataasoowigamig wii-ataasod. Noogiwebin awe daashkiboojigan. Ganabaj giziibwewe... ani-giziibwewebizo. Gii-noonashkine awe gichi-mitig imaa daashkiboojiganing aana-wii-daashkiboonind. Waaboozoog iwidi niimagoojinoog. Odiba'oonaan minik eshamaad ji-onzaamashkinesinid. Miskwaabikizi 'aw dibiki-giizis. Wenipanizi debibinind awe mishtadim. Gichi-gisinaadog igo. Bakwenaamowag igiweg mishtadimoog. Wanapizowag igiw mishtadimoog. Gibaakwa'an daga iwe ishkwaandem. Daki-ayaamagad agwajiing. Gii-madweyaabikise gii-gashkaakwa'igaadeg iwe ishkwaandem. Aabaabika'amawishin nindishkwaandem. Gaawiin aapiji ninzaabaabisii. Bezhig ishkwaandem ningii'-andodamaagen gii-biigonigaadeg gete-waakaa'igan. Ogii-noonde-zaagitoon gaa-onji-ishkodaawaaged. Mii gii-maadizhang i'iw babagiwayaaniigin aana-gii-saagitooyaan. Odaana-gii-saagitoon 'iw ojiimaanensim. Mii 'iw aangwaamas gii-inendang ji-aabajichigaadenig. Waawiikaa na ginaanaagadawenimaa gimishoomisiban. Apane ninaanaagadawenimaa noozhis waasa gaa-dazhi-gikinoo'amawind. Ganabaj ninga-ganoonaa onaagoshig. Naano-mizid akwaakoziwag nindaagimag. Naano-mizid midaaso-mininj nindakooz. Awi-maada'ookiin ini gigishkiganan gaa-piijigaadegin. Zhooshkwa'igan aabaji' wii-shooshkwega'aman gigishkiganan. Aandi ezhi-agooodooyan gigigishkiganan. Bigwadakamig gidaa-izhiwidoonan ogigishkiganan gaa-gii'-maajaad. Megwaa izhiwidaaso awe aawadaatigwed. Gichi-mindido a'awe migizi o'omaa ge-gizhibaayaashid. Aandi endanaakideg gaa-zakideg. Mishawakamig dazhi-niimi'idim. Naadoom giniijaanisens. Giinitam bakitejii'igen. Giinitam ina giwii-kaagiigid? Giinitam oninigen. Giinitam gidaa-oninige. Niwiisagendam nimisad. Mii 'i zhigwa giizhigaadamowaad iwe midewigaan wezhitoowaad. Giimoodam 'a baaka'aakwenh. Biindig awi-gwaabandan nibi. Gii-nibekaazo gii-megwaa-animikiikaag. Gaawiinoon omaa gii'-animikiikaasinoon. Da-besho-biboon omaa. Aaniish enangindeg 'iw odaabaan. Boozitoon iniw makakoon imaa odaabaaning. Gagiizhibaabidewan iniwen odaabaanan gegwejikanidiimagakin. Midaaso-biboon gii-ondaadad indoodaabaanish. Hay', nindoodaabaan gii-kibichise. Biinjaya'ii atewan in... iniwen nibiizikiiganan. Biinjaya'ii imaa gii-izhijiwan. Biinjaya'ii danweweyaange oojiins. Maamawi'idiwag igiweg mindimooyenyag waa-shaabowewaad. Mii 'i zhigwa maamawi'idiwaad igi nikag ozhiitaawaad wii-maajaawaad. Niibinong ningii-gitigaanaanaanig opiniig. Naabizhigan aabajitoon wii'-onizhaman waa'-ozhitooyan. Ningii'-noondawaa awiya bapagotood. Ganabaj nimawadisigoo. Gidaa-mashkikiwaabookawaa. Aaniin epiitenimad awe eshpabid. | Namanj iidog onzaam wayiiba. Ogii-piigoshkaan 'i adoopowinaak gii-apabaadang. Ingii-pi-waabanda'igoo iwe zhizhoobii'igan. Maanaadad. Gaawiin ingii-minwendanziin. Anishaa sa go giwawiyazhinawin ezhichigeyan. Oodenaang ogii-ipizoni'aan omishoomisan. Wegonen apane wenji-nishkaadendang gidaanis. Giishpin aninaatigokaag, giga-iskigamizigemin. Zinigobinidizo gaa-gii'-izhi-wiisagigidigweshing. Agwaaweba'an zhinoodaagan anaamiindim gaa-agwindeg. Aaniin da naa. Gigitim ina. Aaniin apii ge-ashanding. Gii-piindigajigewag gaye wiinawaa gii-ashanding. Biindigeyaawanidiwag waa'-wiisiniwaad. Michi-ashandim omaa noongom. Bigishkishin 'aw diba'igeziswaanens gaa-pangishing. Gichi-goshkwaawaadabi naanaagadawendang. Gaawiin gegoo naanaagadawendanziin awe gaa-onji-bakiiwiid aw gaa-wiikwiid. Agindan endasingin makakoon. Zhebaa ningii'-agindaan nindoozhibii'amaagoowin. Aaniin ezhiwebinang ogiishkiboojigan gii-gawiboojiged. Odanibenaan ina. Hay', mii niin gaawiin indawi-ganawaabisii iwidi waa-inakamigak; onzaam nibiigoshkaa. Weweni imaa ganawaabin. Mii imaa ge-onji-gikendaman ge-izhichigeyan. Wii-kagwejikada'odim noongom gaa-giizhigak. Gidaa-gii'-awi-ganawaabimin gegiinawind. Maagwapidoon gigashkiiwegidaabaan. Ganabaj a'aw minjikaawan gii-kashkigwaazodog. Giishpin waabandaman gijigaanakwagoodeg gii-biboong, wiiba da-gijigadaasin mikwamiing. Gego babaamenimaaken. Maanoo da-ozhiitaa. Gego babaamenimaaken gimishoomis. Megwaa apaakozige. Gego babaamenimaaken awe mindimooyenh. Megwaa bagwa'aaso. Aabitawaabikizi 'aw giizis. Gichi-bagakaasige awe dibiki-giizis aana-aabitawaabikizid. Gichi-bagakaasige awe dibiki-giizis aana-aabitawaabikizid. Mamaandidowag igiw gwiiwizensag. Nindaabajitoon binaakwaan binaakwe'wag nindaanis. Binaakwaan aabajitoon wii-pinaakwe'wad. Hay', gii-maanaagamisin iwe nibi. Gichi-booski-makadewaagamin i'iwe makade-mashkikiwaaboo. Mii 'i gii-ni-maajidaabiid awe aawajidaabaadang ini misan. Aaniin enigokwadeyoonagak? Onibe'aan iniw abinoojiiyensan imaa wewebizoning. Ingii-inaa ji-ikwagoodood iwe wewebizon. Mii zhigwa gegaa naawakweg ji-nawajiiying. Niizhing ningii-pi-nawajiimin gii-bi-bimoseyaang. Gaa-izh-mitanitewang, giga-izhi-nawajiimin; giga-nitiikemin. Debinaak igo gii-izhi-asigisijigaademagad. Indaga shko miinosidoon. Ogii-ikwaabiiginaan iwe nibi imaa moona'ibaaning. Ozaawizi aw gaazhagens. Waabooz waabishkizi gii-biboong; ozaawizi gii-niibing. A'aw abinoojiinh gii-pimose imaa azhashkiing ezhi-wiinizided. Azhashkiikaang gii-ishkwaa-gimiwang, mii imaa niin ako waabamagwaa. Ingii-odaapinige iwidi gii-pagijigeng. Ogichi-apiitendaan gaa-ina'oonind gii-odaapiniged imaa gii-pagijigeng. Gichi-gabeya'ii mawi a'aw abinoojiinh. Indaga o-waabam. Niizho-biboonagad gii-waabamag ishkwaaj nishiime. Mii iwidi gii-waabamag waawaashkeshi jiigaakwaa. Niminwendaan waabaminaan. Daga izhiwizhishin aakoziiwigamigong. Niwii-wi-waabamaa mashkikiiwinini. Nindaakoz. Ningii'-mitinigoo gii-gimoodiyaan odaabaan. Mii dash omaa wenji-namadabiyaan biindig gibaakwa'odiiwigamigong. Gii-aanjichigaade iwe gibaakwa'odiiyigamig. Dibikong gii-kwanabibizowag niizh ininiwag. Bezhig gegaa gii'-nisaabaawe. Mii zhigwa bimiinowaad igi nikag. Mii 'i gikendaagwak oshki-dagwaaging. Gii-pimwewidamoog igi nikag. Bimaabiigamo'idiwag nikag. Giiniboozh gidoozhibii'iganaak. Ningiishka'ise endaso-dagwaagi. Wiinge naa onzaamibidewan naabikwaanensan gabe-giizhik. Bedowe gaagiigidod a'awe inini. Gotaamigwad aapiji. Miskwaabiigwakonese 'iw waasigan. Mii imaa endazhiikewaad igi abinoojiinyag imaa zhooshooshkobizonikaaning. Zhaabonigan obimiwidoon waabizheshi. Babaamikawe imaa waabizheshi. Naanan ningii-piinaag waabizheshiwag. Zhebaa dash gakina ningii-pakonaag, miinawaa ningii-shiiba'waag. Naawiskatig ningii-ininawaa amik. Diba'igiiziswaan gidibaabamaa epiichi-giizhigak. Onzaam bejibizo a'aw diba'igiiziswaan. Aandi awe diba'igiiziswaan. Omaa ningii-asaaban. Weweni ganawendamog 'i minisi ebiitamong. Giishpin ani-wanibizod, wiikaa baamaa da-dagoshin gaa-izhi-andawendaagozid. Andawendaagozi Richard ji-ozhitood wanii'ige-waakaa'igaans. Ikogaabawin imaa. Mii omaa inagakeyaa ge-bi-izhidaabaajigaadeg i'iwe gichi-adoopowin. Indawaaj indikogaabaw imaa jibwaa-anokii'igooyaan. Mamaangibagizi wiigobaatig. Nimaamaa ogii-andawaabamaan iniw wiigobaatigoon. Miish imaa gii-ozhitood iniwen negwaakwaanan. Ayi'ii ogii-aabajitoon iw waagaakwadoons. Gego odaminwaadangen i'i ishkode. Giga-zhigingwaam. Aaniin epiitading. Godikwa'an epiitading zaaga'igan. Aanii zhigwa epiitading. Mii na 'i zhigwa ji-gii-pimaadagaakoyangoban. Giinawind giga-ozhiga'igemin. Bakwenemagadini ina owe okijiwaabik. Waanda-bakwene naa agwajiing 'iw. Niwaanda-wiinishkiinzhigwe naa. Ishkwekana madwe-badakizo mitig. Mamaandaawichigewinini ogii-naagotoon iwe gichi-biiminakwaan ji-bazigwiimagadinig. Gii-shagashkii gii-gaagiimaa'aad zhiishiiba'. Mii go naasaab ena'adood iniwen bema'anaad. Gii-pabiiwishkam awe waawaashkeshi gaa-... gaa-pima'anag. Gii-niigose aw ombaakwa'igan gaa-onji-niisiseg aana-gii-ombaakwa'amaan. Aapiji ginoosagad nindadoopowinaak. Onandomaamaan awe inday iniw gaa-pi-odishiyangid dibikong. Gidaa-gagwe-odisaa. Ani-bagakaabang giga-bi-odisininim. Besho omaa daawag igi anishinaabeg. Gii-onakiiwag igi anishinaabeg. Akawe ninookagwinjidoon waawaashkeshiwizagiinens jibwaa-biindaabika'amaan. Gaye wiinawaa iidog wii-ashangewag. Awenenag eshangewaad. Ogii-wanitoon i'iw omiskodoonechigan awe oshki-ikwe. Meshkod giga-diba'amawin wiiji'iyan. Giishpin ganage bebangii diba'amawid endaso-giizis, maagizhaa ingoding indaa-gii-izhi-diba'amaag. Zhooshkwa'iganaatigong izhi-bakijiigisidoon waa-shooshkwega'aman. Babigozigwaa gii-ziigwang. Gaawiin gidaa-zhooshkwaada'esii. Babaamibatooyaan niwiisagendaanan nikaadan. Bebakaan igi mitigoog izhinaagoziwag. Aanawi go aana-waawiindamowaad, mii go gaawiin nisidotanziiwan. Mii go aanawi gii-minoshing a'awe majiikiwis imaa ziindaamagak. Mii go aanawi gii-ombishkaad awe bakwezhigan gaa-onadinag. Aanawi go naa weweni ningii'-waawiindamawaa. Gego izhinoo'waaken giiji-bimaadizii aanawi go gii-bizhishigwaabikak. Amikotawagaang inigokobagiziwag mitigoog, mii apii gaa-wiikongeng. Nimaamaa ogii-aabajitoon mitigo-negwaakwaan gii-ozhiga'waad iniwen mitigoon. Gizibiiga'an daga iwe waabishkiigin. Wiinad. Wiinad i'iw adoopowinaak. Mii na go ji-biinitooyamban? Wiinadoon gidoonaaganan. Gidaa-giziibiiginaanin. Baabige naa aabita-niibing gii-ojijise. Gii'-agaashiinyensi nindaanikoobijigan gaa-gii'-nitaawiigid. Gii'-niso-dibaabiishkoojiganezi eta awashime. Agaamishkode danawazo nimishoomis. Jiigishkode nindanawaz. Aaniish ezhichigaanaad ini dewe'iganan. Gichi-zaasaakwe awe mindimooyenh epiichi-jiikimigod iniw dewe'iganan miinawaa negamonid. Ogii'-niimikaan gii-dibishkamoo-nagamo'ind. Onzaam babiiwaawan ini zhiishiibanwiinsan. Babiiwaawan makizinan. Gaawiin nindebishkanziinan. Endaso-dibik iko ninganawaabandaan nimazinaatesijigan. Endaso-dibik nindataage endaayaan. Ogii-saagijinizhikawaan iniw abinoonjiiyan neshiwanaadakamigizinid. Aaniin apii ge-ashanding. Aaniin apii ge-izhiwidamowad obaashkizigan. Ningii-kagwejimaa nimaamaa aaniin apii ge-bagamibideg i'iw booziwe-odaabaan. Aaniin dash apii waa'-maajii-gitigeyan. Aaniin apii waa'-maadanokiiyan waabang. Wewayiiba ndamajise. Aapiji mino-dibikad. Mii go wenda-giizhigaateg. Mii 'i gii-maadaasing iwe bimaasijigan gaa-bakiseg. Ogii-naada'oodoon iwe manoominike-jiimaanens gaa-maadaasininig. Indaga niizhozid biidamawishin awe mekadewaabiigizid zenibaa. Ogii-kwiinawendaan 'iw gaa-andawendang gaa-onji-mindawed. Indawaaj igo inga-baapi'aa awe gaa-mindawed aanawi agwaa'izekwed miinawaa. Bijiinag ninga-ozhi'aa a'aw bakwezhigan. Mii dash onadinag. Gabe-biboon iwidi gii-anokii nishiime. Gaawiin dash geyaabi anokiisiin Ingii-wiisin niin zhigwa. Giin dash. Aandi dash wendakaaneziyin. Aaniin dash wenji-mawiyan. Awenen dash gaa-wiijayaawad iwidi gii-wi-ayaayin. Giishpin gashkitooyan, gidaa-ojibwewibii'ige ji-wiindamaageyin aaniin apii ge-zagaswe'idiing. Gaawiin ganabaj nindaa-izhaasii. Bebangii nindashamaag igiw abinoojiinyag ozhaashi-manoomin. Gaawiin ganabaj ominwendanziinaawaa. Gaawiin ganabaj indaa-debwetawaasii gaa-gii-kagwejimid wii'-wiidigemid. Ningii'-noondawaa "gaawiin" ikidod. Gaawiin ganabaj odaa-gashkitoon. Biiwaabiko-giishkiboojiganens gidaa-aabajitoon ji-bookwaabikiboonad gashkaabika'igan giishpin gii-wanitooyan gidaabaabika'igan. Gaawiin ganage indaa-anoonaasii awe goopadizid. Gibi-anoonin ji-odaabii'iwetamawiyan. Gidanoonigoo ji-o-wiindaman i'iw oshki-aazhogan. Mii imaa bimiwidaasod awe gaa-anoonind ji-naadid ini aabajichiganan. Gii-pi-anoonaa ji-o-ganawendaawasod awe niwiijiiwaagan. Nindanoonig ji-ozhibii'igetamawag wii-kagwe-anokiid ji-mooshkinebii'amawag mazina'igan. Aana-onji'agwaa igiw abinoojiinyag, onjida miigaadiwaad. Odoonji'aan ji-niminaakosinig gii-naniizaanak zaaga'igan. Noopimiing ninoondawaa madwewe'od bine. Gabe-biboon noopimiing ningiishka'aakwe. Waasa noopimiing odoondaawanaawaa' asinii' gaa-madoodiswaagewaad. Gidaa-agimaag igiweg nemaabiinsag. Odasigishimaan onemaabiinsiman. Aandi wiin endaad. Ambe daga da-agwaataawag igiw abinoonjiinyag. Mii go gegaa gabe-ishkwaa-naawakwe zaagagwamowaad imaa nibiikaang. Gii-ziigwang agwaataawag miskwaadesiwag gii-ando-owaawanowaad. Ani-agwaataa amik babaa-ando-wiisinid noopimiing. Gego baashkizwaaken noozhe-mooz gii-aamanoozowaad. Mamaangiminagiziwag igi mishiiminag gaa-piinagwaa. Onzaamiinowag mishiiminag. Ogii'-agaasikonaan mishiiminan jibwaa-amwaad. Aapiji biichaa onigam gaa-gii'-izhi-gabadoowaang; aabitoonigam ningii'-ani-bagijinige. Aanind binesiwag ozaawishkiinzhigwewag. Debitaagoziwag igiw binesiwag iwidi giizhigong. Gizhiiwe awe binesi noondaagozid. Ingii-segimig awe gaa-pabaamwewidang binesi awasonaago. Zhaawanong ondwewebizowag binesiwag. Giishpin ningizigodeg, wiiba gigizheb giga-gagwe-aazhawagaakomin. Giziibweweshkaa awe ditibidaabaanens: onzaam agwaagwaabikishin. Wiinitamawaa da-owi-bagida'waawag. Wiinitamawaa da-nibinaadiwag. Wiinitamawaa da-agwaa'amawaawag gaa-nagamowaad. Wawenabi waa-tanagindang dibaajimoo-mazina'igan. Gaawiin wikaa ingoji gii-izhiwinaasii wenji-goshiweshkid abinoojiinyens. Odizhiwinaan oosan iwidi Bemijigamaag Daga izhiwizhishin aakoziiwigamigong. Niwii-wi-waabamaa mashkikiiwinini. Nindaakoz. Iwidi inagakeyaa izhiwizh. Gii'-izhiwinaa mindimoowenh gaa-bwaanawi'od gaa-dazhi-niimi'idiwind. Zhiibaa-nibewin izhiwebishkan gimakizinan. Ganabaj ninga-azhe-giiwewidoon. Gaawiin nindaa-debishkanziin. Ninga-meshkodoonaan. Makadewiingwe a'awe gechi-wiinaanagiingwed. Noosiban ogii'-minopidaan biisi-manoomin. Gaawiin ningoji niwii-izhaasii noongom gaa-giizhigak. Ningoji go niiyo-diba'iganeyaag ninga-bi-dagoshin. Gii-paakaakosin i'iw waasechigan gabe-dibik. Gii-piindigese a'aw obikwaanaajiinh. Gego gabeya'ii zheyaakonangen ishkwaandem. Da-biindigesewag zagimeg. Ogii-nibiikaadaan i'iwe noomazhaan wenji-jiikaakiziged. Nimoonenimaa go awe gegwaanisagi-onzaamidooned. Ganabaj jiikaakizige. Ozhooshkwega'aan ogiboodiyegwaazon. Zhooshkwa'iganaatigong izhi-bakijiigisidoon waa-shooshkwega'aman. Ningii'-awi-mawadisaa nookomis zhebaa. Wiinge go ani-oziigiingwe. Gichi-aya'aawi. Ogidadewenamoog abinoojiinyag gaa-gaakaazootaadiwaad. Ingii-piminizhikawaa inday gaa-niimandang niwiiwakwaan. Agaamikana iwidi debinaagozi endwewemad. Ginandwewemigoo. Gii-wiisagise omisadaang zhebaa. Ningozis ogii-kanawendaan endaayaan gii-mawadishiweyaan. Baanimaapii ninga-mawadishiwe. Niwiizhaamig wii-mawadishiwed. Endasonaagosh nimawadishiwe. Ayaapii go gii-niisijiwan iwe miikana. Weweni go bimibizoniken. Jiikaagamin iwe aniibiish. Weweni ogii-minwaagamitoon. Onaabandan weweni iwe waa-mamooyan. Memwech igo weweni wii'-wiisini. Wakewan i'iw akwaandawaagan. Weweni. Weweni odaminog. Weweni gidaa-naanaagadawendam waa'-izhichigeyan. Weweni inanjige'idizon. Gego miijiken gaa-boozaag. Gidaa-bi-giziisaginamaw ina? Wiinisagaani endaad nookoo. Niwii'-awi-giziisaginamawaa. Babaaminizhikodaadiwag igiweg abinoonjiiyag bepeshinidiwaad. Indaga imaa ani-noogishkaan. Ninoonde-zaaga'am. Mii imaa gii-noogishkaawaad igiw biiwideg imaa endaashiyaan Mii omaa gii-pimi-noogishkaad awe mindimooyenh gaa-pabaamigamigwed. Mii imaa oshki-noogishkaawigamigong gii-pi-noogishkaad awe gaa-shigajibii'ag bijiinaago. Nimaanishkaag zhiiwi-bakwezhigan. Gaawiin geyaabi bagidanaamosii. Ningii'-nisaabaawanaa amik. Gigii-wanigwaas ina? Mii imaa dibendaagoziyaan dewe'iganing niniigaani-niimi'iwewininiw. Agaawaa deba'oode zaga'igan; onzaam michaabikad. Ikosidamaw ge-izhi-onabid. Maagoshkoodoon gidagwana'igan ji-baakiwebaasinzinog. Ningii-noondese giziindime'on. Ningii-wi-adaawen gii-maa'ishkamaan. Dagosidoon ashkaatigoon omaa biindig. Ogii-tagosidoon gookooshiwi-wiiyaas gii-bigishkiboodood moozo-wiiyaas Aasamajiw debinaagoziwag wiigwaasaatigoog. Gii-naabidoo'igaadeni iwe obasikwepizon. Wiineta go agwaa'amaazo. Ininamaw odoonaagan ji-agwaa'amaazod. Mii go bezhigwan: animaapi, ani-baapi. Bemijigamaag indaana-gii-izhaa andawanokiiyaan. Gii-mikwanokii awe gaa-izhaad Bemijigamaag gii-andawanokiid. Megwaa bimosed a'aw inini gaa-izhi-gawised. Ezhi-gawised naa a'aw mitig ezhi-wiisagishkoozod naa nisayenh. Odaasonaan 'iw akwaandawaagan. Noonashkine; onzaam ginwaa. Agaasademon onigam. Aapiji da-baatemagad noongom ji-niibing. Gego mashi biindigeken. Geyaabi nibiiwisagaa. Noongom nindishkwaa-giziisaginige. Aaniin ezhi-wiinzod awedi ikwe nemadabid. Bagandiz gii-izhi-wiinzo a'awe ikwe gaa-wiiidigemaad ini "Captain John Smith" gaa-inimind. Doodooshaaboo imaa ningii-atoon dakisijiganing. Dakisijiganing izhi-atoon gaa-gii'-ishkwandaman ji-wanaajisinzinog. Gomaa go inigokwaa nindakisijigan. Gigoshkoz ina. Noomaya go mayaawabi. Mii bijiinag gii-goshkozid. Gigizheb inga-goshkoz waabang. Ogii-kashkiiginaan oniijaanisensan wii'-nibe'aad. Gii-goshkozinid ogii'-aabiiginaan. Gidaa-basindibeganaamaa giishpin bizindanzig. Giishpin biijimaamad giniijaanis ganabaj wiiyaanziye. Gii'-miijinidizo. Daga ningodonaagaans naazikamawishin nitii ge-minikweyaan. Aaniin epiitagoodooyan gima'iingani-nagwaaganan. Agoode mazinaakizowin imaa aasamisagong. Minwapikaade apikaanashk gaa-agoodeg biinjidaabaan. Biijibiisaa o'owe ba-agoodeg aanakwad. Gichi-ajina gii-pimi-noogishkaa awe ingos. Ojaanimishkaa iwidi wii-tagoshing ezhaad. Aasamaabik mazinaabikinigan naagwad. Wenda-aabidwewidam a'awe gookooko'oowish. Gigizheb ningii-onishkaa gii-piindaakoojigeyaan. Indaga onishkaan. Mii iwe wayiiba ji-bi-dagoshing awe wepaazid. Naaningoding eta go ningaganoonaa. Gichi-gigizhebaawii. Mii go bijiinag noongom gigizhebaawiiyaan owe giziibiigisaginigewi-giizhigak. Bookwaabikiboodoon zaga'igan giishpin onzaam ginwaabikak. Baasige-makakong izhi-biina'an gegoo wii-paasaman. Andawaabandan misan jibwaa-dibikak. Giga-giikajingwaamomin. Ogii-pwaanawitoon aana-gagwe-nagajimaandang imaa endazhi-bigishkanimaagwadinig. Mii go onjida odinaadiziwin ji-gwiishkoshaabide-nagamod gegoo izhichiged a'awe nimishoome. Obiminizha'aan mino-inaadiziwin. Aaniindi ezhaayin. Akawe bii'ishin. Oodenaang niwii-izhaa Awasonaago ningii-izhaa gichi-oodenaang. Biinizikaa ni-maajaa ninaabem. Dibi ezhaagwen. Giinetawaa izhaag iwidi andomigooying. Omaa bi-izhaan. Indaga dawinamaw 'iw desa'on aw niningwan. Mii imaa ge-izhi-bagidoomaad iniw waawaashkeshiwan. Omashkikiikaadaan i'iw ogidig gaa-bishagisidood. Omadwegamizaan i'iw wiishkobaaboo awe eskigamiziged. Gabaya'ii zhigwa ondendi awe naadoobiid iwe wiishkobaaboo. Mii iwe gii-mookiid awe gaa-aapidazina'iged imaa adaawewigamigong. Anaamakamig gii-onji-mookii a'aw obiigomagakii Gii-ishkwaa-gimiwang nookaabaawe aki. Mii apii mookiiwaad mooseg. Akakojiishi gii'-mookii. Agaamashkiig nitaawiginoon mashkiigiminan. Awanjish ogii-maandandaan iwe dekaag aana-dewaabided. Gii-naajimiijimeyaan ingii-adaawen dekaag. Ogii-nagaji'aan iniw odayan gegwaanisagizinid gaa-onji-wenipanizhi'aad. Gii-maniseyaan niibowa ningii-kawa'waag mitigoog. Gaawiin abisii. Megwaa babaamaadizi. Gaawiin da-wenipanasinoon. Gaawiin niminwendanziin gaa-wiisagang. Mii gaawiin gijipizosii a'awe gaa-pangisijiged. Zhagashkaanaamik izhi-bagidaabiin. Indaga o-wewebaabiigin 'a abinoojiinyens debwewidang. Gaawiin wikaa ingoji gii-izhiwinaasii wenji-goshiweshkid abinoojiinyens. Ganabaj ingii-maanadaawe gii-ayaamaan ini makizinan. Bezhig michaamagad. Ingii-maanadaawe gii-naanag awe mish... mishtadimozhish. Gii-mamaanjigoowizi eyedawinik. Migoshkaajise awe waasamoowidaabaan aana-gii-adaaweyaan. Gichi-mayaginaagozi awe mizhakojiishi enimibatood. Ningii-tebaabamaa gaa-mitaaskiiwe-bagizod. Mii imaa wenji-wanitood i'iw obiimaskwa'iganim. Ingii-noondaan madwesing iwidi niisaya'ii. Aabitawigaad akobii gii-aazhawaadagaaziid. Giga-waabamaanaan bimi-aazhawaadagaaziid awiya. Gibaakwa'an ishkwaandem iwidi ataasoowigamigong. Ingii-noondam gii-pazhined. Gigii'-noondam ina gaa'-inakamigak gichi-oodenaang? Giizhaa ningii'-noondam wii-pi-gichi-izhiwebak bijiinaago. Gii-noondam wii-maawanjii'inding wenji-ozhiitaad iwidi gaye wiin wii-izhaad. Awasaya'ii iwidi ogii-atoon. Gii-shiigosin giziibiiga'igani-makakosag omaa gaa-ayateg. Aaniin da naa aapidakamig ezhiwebak. Aaniin ezhiwebak agwajiing? Gagwanisagakamig naa gaa-izhiwebak. Gegoo iwidi izhiwebad awasisag. Babaamaadodan gaa-izhiwebak. Mii go 'iw gabe-giizhig ge-izhiwebak ji-babimibiisaag. Ondendam 'i gaa-izhiwebadinig bijiinaago. Babaa-moona'ibii awe moona'ibiiwinini. Odazhiikawaan odasabiin. Omegwaa-bagwa'waan. Atoobaaning ngii-siiginaamin i'iw ozhiga'iganaaboo gii-naadoobiiyaan ani-onaagoshig. Mii iwidi a... ategin biinichiganan anaamaya'ii atoobaaning. Weweni go izhinaagozi a'aw atoobaan. Gonige ogii'-nisidotaan gaa-gii'-izhibii'amawag. Gonige gidaa-awi' midaaswaabik. Gonige aabawaadog. Awanjish gii-niminaadagaako awe gaa-twaashing aana-gii-kina'amawind. Gii-sagakisijige awe indikwem gaa-ishkwaakamigak. Naanaagadawaabam ezhichiged. Anaamakamig aanind daawag awesiinyensag. Ganabaj aanind biskanechigaansag jaagizowag wenji-maazhibideg 'iw odaabaan. Aanind eta go. Aanind eta go gii'-ando-bagizowag gii-ani-onaagoshig. Aanind gaawiin gegoo omaa atesinoon gey-aabajitooyangoban. Ningii-kanawaabamigoog igi abinoojiinyag ozhibii'igeyaan Bekaa niwii-ozhibii'ige jibwaa-maajaaying. Mii go apii gaa-aabiziingwashid gii-andonaad owiipemaaganan. Mii go gii-aabiziingwashiyaan. Ingii-te-nibaa. Aaniin dash enagoodood. Biinichigewag imaa eyedawikana. Awasigamig danakamigad. Ingii-andomaag igiw abinoojiinyag  ji-bi-odaminowaad. Mii iniw gaa-andawenimaad ji-bi-gaagiigidonid gaa-onji-andomaad. Ingii-andomigoo idi aakoziwiiwigamigong. Gii-shaabwaakizigaade nikaakigan. Gego indawaaj andomaaken awe. Maji-mashkiki 'a eta go ogikendaan. Bijiinaago ningii-kinisinaa'ogomin agaami-zaaga'igan onzaam gii'-mamaangaashkaa. Baamaa waabang giga-bi-naazikawin. Naagaj baamaa giga-dazhiikaamin. John wii-ni-giiwebizo noongom ishkwaa-naawakwenig. John gii-kiiwebizo zhebaa. Indaashaan. Omaa bi-onabin. Apabiwin nindaabajitoon onabiyaan wiisiniyaan. Onabig imaa naawisag. Inoo'amaw inakeya'ii ge-izhi-onabid. Nimazinigwaadaan i'iw babagiwayaan. Gidaa-bagwa'aan ina ow nibabagiwayaan. Giwii-piizikaan ina iwe babagiwayaan gemaa... gemaa go iwedi. Indaga maajinizha'an iwe maajiibii'igan. Ogii-maajinizha'aan bijiinaago 'i gaa-tazhiikang anokii-mazina'igan. Ingii-sanagi'ig awe gaa-maajiidood indoodaabaan. Anaamisagong gii-izhi-zhegoode. Mii iwidi gii-noogibizod jiigigamig. Gii-kibozigwajiwag amikwag. Agaawaa gii-te-mizhagaa; gegaa gii-kibozigwaji. Gegaa ningii'-ozhaashibiz gii-bi-giiwebizoyaan. Mii ko o'ow waabooyaan naa asemaan asaad da-bagijiged awiya. Gaye giinawind gigii-igoomin ji-bagijigeying. Ogichi-apiitendaan gaa-ina'oonind gii-odaapiniged imaa gii-pagijigeng. Gii-kwiinawi-doodam aana-wii-wiidookaazod omaa o-bagijigewind. Niibiwa na giin gidayaan waasigani-bimide. Niibiwa diba'amawaa gaa-gikinoo'amaaged. Ogidaatig namadabi 'aw omakakii. Gii-mashkawaabiigad i'iw zhinoodaagan gaa-aabajichigaadeg gii-dakobinind a'aw asab. Namanj igo. Bizaan-ayaa wa'awe. Naawikwam awi-dwaa'igen. Waagaakwad aabadad gii-dwaa'igeng, maagizhaa gaye eshkan. Giishpin ditisadowed gidamikwayaan, gaawiin aapiji daa-aginzosii. Gii-ziigwang binadowe animosh. Ditisadowe gii-niibininig. Ombiigweyaakwa'ige meme mitigong. Meme miskotigwaane, makadewikoozhe, gaye makadewaawigane. Giga-aabaaka'amoon iwe ataasoowigamig giishpin wendamiziwanen. Ogii-tawisidoon ataasoowigamig wii-ataasod. Gaawiinoon omaa gii'-animikiikaasinoon. Da-besho-biboon omaa. Agaawaa go naagoziwag anangoog; ganabaj wiiba da-zoogipon. Eniwek gii-aabawaa-dibikad, mii eta go gii-aabitawazhed. Aaniin ekoosagak. Bwaawishkaa odaabaanaak. Ganabaj onzaam magozigoshin. Obishagibinaan iniwen wezaawiminagizinid. Gii'-ani-mikawi. Ani-aabiziishin. Ogii-tebibidoon jiimaan jibwaa-niminaaweyaasininig. Gego babaamenimaaken animoshag gaa-miigaadiwaad. Giga-bitamigoog. Naadwewem mooz. Opimeya'ii ani-inaaboonodaa. Aaniin epiichaag oodenaang? |  Niisimidana daso-diba'igan apiichaa. Eyiidawitawag gibishe. Mooz animibatoo. Jiigaakwaang ani-apatoo. Odapenimonan omaamaayan ji-bami'igod. Weweni obami'aan iniw omishoomisan. Niibaa-anokii gii-anokii'ind. Indawaaj indikogaabaw imaa jibwaa-anokii'igooyaan. Bwaawidam ge wiin ji-anokii'ind. Aaniin endashiwaad. Mii go 'i minik endashid a'awe bebinezid bakwezhigan. Atoon daga iniw onaaganan imaa ataasowining. Aandi gaa-onjiwidood iniw biizikiiganan. Aaniin wenji-wiiweginaman iniw mazina'iganan. Bebesho badakidewan iniw wiigiwaaman. Anaamaabikong atewan iniw aabaabika'iganan. Niin iko ningii-kidinamegwe binda'ogowaad igi giigoonyag. Mii iw nisogon aabidaanimak. Gaawiin ganage gibitaanimasinoon. Indaga okaaden awe wezhiitaad waa-o-naaniimid. Biiwaabiko-giishkiboojiganens gidaa-aabajitoon ji-bookwaabikiboonad gashkaabika'igan giishpin gii-wanitooyan gidaabaabika'igan. Aandi ezhitigweyaag. Mii iwidi gaa-pimi-izhitigweyaag 'i ziibi jiigikana. Waasa izhitigweyaa. Anooj izhitigweyaa i'iw ziibi. Ate biindoonag i'iw makakosag. Wiinad imaa biinji-makakosagong. Aniibiishaaboo wiishkobaagamin. Gabe-dibik ogii-takagonjidoon odoodooshaaboom. Awasisag iwidi namadabi awe endwewemad. Ningikenimaa iwidi ayaad. Ninoondawaa megaded. Zagwakidewan manoominaganzhiin. Bwaawishkaa jiimaan. Bagoshi'iwe ji-ashamind. Gii-migoshkaadendam gaa-ako-wani'aad iniw ojiwaaman. Odoonizhwaa' giigoonya' waa'-nametegokaanaad. Biinish igo ani-agaasinaagozi migizi gaa-ishpaashid. Oshkiniigikweg iwidi mawinzowag noopiming. Mii go apane naawakweshin aw oshkiniigikwens. Minwanaamo. Ganabaj wii'-ani-mino-ayaa. Maagwaakwa'an ji-banaskwaagisesinog. Nimaagwaakwa'aanan wiigwaasi-makako-waakaayaagibijigan. Ogii-ozaawaakizwaan iniw giboziganan waa-amwaad. Gichi-agwaagoshi awe giboziganish. Indaga owi-webin. Awenen waa'-ozaawaakizwaad giboziganan. Midaaswi awiyag gidaa-ashamaanaanig. Omaanaadodaan iwe waa-izhi-biinjwebinigetamaaged. Obishagibinaan iniwen wezaawiminagizinid. Gabe-giizhik abaabasan miinan wii-paasiminikeyan. Wegonen ebaabasaman. Ondaabate giwaaginogaan. Bijiinaago gii-shakaagonagaag, nindede gii'-miikanaake. Noongom wawiinge baapaagadamon. Obookoshkawaa' odaagima'; onzaam zhakaagonagaa. Gidoobizhikiim ina. Gii-sagaswe'iwe awe ogimaa anda-gikendang enaasamiiying Gii-ishkweyaange awe gaa-onji-metasikawaad ini odoogimaaman. Wii-asigi'idiwag igiweg ogimaag wii-tazhindamowaad iwe odaakewin. Giishpin mikawad asin gayaashaabikizid, gidaa-bakada'igaagenan. Babiiskijiitaa babaa-ayaad. Nookizo a'aw waabooz. Aaniin epiitweweg ishkodewidaabaan ba-noondaagwak. Gii'-noondaagwad gaa-wiisakweg dibikong. Ganabaj gegaa gigii-pisikaagonaan bisibisidoosh. Oshki-adaawewigamigong gii-ondadaawe i'iw zhiiwitaagani-gookoosh. Ziigaasin gimanoominim. Ingii-izhaamin imaa apagajwebiniganing. Gichi-wiikaa gii-angomaagwad apii gaa-pi-maajaayaang. Naawaakigan ogii-sagamigoon ezigaan. Onzaamiinowag noongom gaa-niibing ezigaag. Midaaso-diba'igaans gii-izhise. Ashi-naano-diba'iganens izhiseg giga-wiisinimin. Ayaapiichinaag izhaa Njaan banaskwiiwigamigong, giishpin gitimisig. A'aw abinoojiinh gii-pimose imaa azhashkiing ezhi-wiinizided. Ganabaj gegoo inaapine awe gidayinaan. Mii gosha wanitood obiiwayan. Aaniin enaapined? Anooj izhitigweyaa i'iw ziibi. Anooj igo indinaabandam. Anaamisagong gii-izhi-zhegoode. Ayi'ii dash ogii-aabajitoon biskitenaagan gii-atood imaa onjigaanid ini mitigoon. Onjigaawag mitigoog. Ningaagonaasowag. Awenen dinowa bineshiinh gaa-noondaagozid? Noondaagoziwag manidoog. Wiisakwe gaakaabishiinh noondaagozid. Ombiigiziwag igiweg gaagaagiwag noondaagoziwaad. Giishpin gaye diindiisi noondaagozid, dibaajimo wii'-ani-aabwaag. Biinjitawag gii-piindoodewan iniwen zagimen. Baapaawin 'a goon maa gibabiinzikawaaganing. Aaniin epogwak. Gii-paashkinese i'iw akakanzhe i'iwidi gii-izhi-ziigwebinamaan. Gabeya'ii nigii-kanawaabamaag igi waagoshensag babaa-gaagiiwaapiwaad. Gego gabeya'ii zheyaakonangen ishkwaandem. Da-biindigesewag zagimeg. Ogii-kojitoon iwe oshki-wewebanaabaan gaa-adaawed. Odaadowebishkaan obiinzikawaagan; onzaam agaasiigadini. Ningii'-mitinigoo gii-gimoodiyaan odaabaan. Mii dash omaa wenji-namadabiyaan biindig gibaakwa'odiiwigamigong. Nagwaaganeyaabiin indoonagoodoonan. Ogii-maanagoodoon 'i nagwaaganeyaab awe weshki-agoodood. Aasamaateshim gidamikwayaan ji-baasod. Gii-minomaanjige imaa jiibaakwewigamigong ondaabatenig. Onaabikaan onik. Onzaam wiikaa gigii'-wiindamaagoomin waa'-izhichigewaad. Zagwakidewan manoominaganzhiin. Bwaawishkaa jiimaan. Aandi endanweweg. | Awasi-gakiiw danwewe. Wanako-niminaawaandawaagan danwewewan. Ogii-piimaskonaan 'iw zagaakwa'igan gii-mashkawaakwa'ang. Nimaanendam enaajimotawid. Ambe ani-maajaadaa. Andookomaazh. Aaniin enaabadizid awe odaabaan gaa-abid idi mashkikiiwigamigong. Mii na awe aakoziiwidaabaan. Mii 'iw bijiinag gii-nanaa'endang gaa-oko-gwayakobii'igaadenig obiindigajigan. Gii-noonashkine awe makwa aana-wii-piindigeyooded imaa waanzhing. Ondamizi awe endwewemad. Megwaa-ozhitamaage iwidi bakejiigaan. Mii go iwidi gaa-ina'adooyaan dibikong gii-izhaayaan. Gaagiidaawigane awe gaa-izhiiwiid mitigoon gii-tazhiikawaad bijiinaago. Miskwaabikide iwe biiwaabik. Ogii-pwaanawitoon aana-gagwe-nagajimaandang imaa endazhi-bigishkanimaagwadinig. Gii-onzaamibizowag imaa washkamonig igiw gaa-anibesewaad. Gii-onzaamibizo gaa-onji-biigwaasidood 'i badagwana'igan Gii-onzaamibizo gaa-onji-bakobiibizod. Aapiji go agaasitaagozi, maagizhaa abinoojiinh. Gaa-goshkosed igo naa awe gechi-onzaamigaamod. Odaapinan gaa-ozaawibagak aniibiish. Biindigen. Gego memwech madweyaakwa'igeken. Onzaam dakwaakozi 'aw biindasaagan... ji-aabaji'agiban. Makade-ozaawadowewag amikwag, ningoding gaye waabishkadowewag. Giga-aabaaka'amoon iwe ataasoowigamig giishpin wendamiziwanen. Giishpin ondamiziyan, niin giga-ozhibii'igetamawin. Wiindamawishin waa'-ikidoyan. Aandi enaashid. Baapi'idiwag dazhimaawaad ogete-wiinimoshenyiwaan. Daabida iniwe gaa-mikomaawaad. Ogii-mikomaan iniw ogete-wiiwan. Wiinishin a'aw giziingwe'on. Niwani-bagidinaag ningiziingwe'onag. Weweni ozagakiiginaa' ogiziingwe'ona' gaa-paasonid. Eyedawaya'ii agwapidewan. Ninandawendam ji-bimosemagak anishinaabemowin. Andawendam ji-miinind zhooniyaan waa'-awi'aazod imaa zhooniyaawigamigong. Aaniin enaandeg. Ogii-piimaskonaan 'iw zagaakwa'igan gii-mashkawaakwa'ang. Giishpin mikwaminaaniwang, waabowayaan gidaa-badagwana'waa gidoodaabaan ji-maakishkoozosig. Gii-takakamigaabaawe dibikong gii-gimiwang. Ganabaj gii'-mikwaminaaniwan. Minweweshin mikwam ogidabak gii-mikwaminaaniwang. Noonashkine; onzaam ginwaa. Ogidaatig nanaamadabi bizhiins. Gichi-nanaamadabi naanaagadawendang miinawaa bagosendang ji-mizhakwadinig. Gibichibiisaag, apii agwajiing imaa niwii-o-nanaamadab. Wawiinge gichi-nanaamadabiwag igiweg enwebiwaad. Gaawiin gegoo inaabadizisii; onzaam nibaashki. Anaamaya'ii gii-inaabi andawaabandang ogiboodiyegwaazon. Daga sa naa inaabin ezhaayang, Giga-bitaabikishinimin. Ingii-waabamaa baa-aabitoojiinaad. Naazibiiwidoon waasigani-bimide-atoobaanan. Maagizhaa waabang ninga-bakwezhiganaabookaadan nooka'iiwagwaan. Mamigobidoon nooka'iiwagwaan gaa-mashkawaakwading, aanind wii-siiginaman gijiibaakwaanakikong. Ishkwandamawishiyok nooka'iiwagwaan. Gonige gidaa-awi' midaaswaabik. Gitwen igo odawi'aan zhooniyaan. Ogii-niigosidoon indoodaabaanish aana-gii-awi'ag. Azhenamaagen ziinzibaakwad gaa-gii'-awi'igooyan. Gii-minwaatese i'iwe gaa-o-ganawaabandamaang mazinaatesijigan i'imaa godagiing. Ozazegaatoon owaakaa'igan gii-gichi-anama'egiizhigak. Minwaateseni. Nagabisagoog okwaakoshinoog. Mitakamig onji-zaagikweni akakojiishi. Bagoneyaanike akakojiishi waa'-onji-biindiged endaad. Akakojiishi gii'-mookii. Naawagaam madwe-agomo maang. Weweni ganawendaagwad iwe zhooniyaa-makakoons etemagak. Mary miinawaa Rose nagaji'idiwag ezhichigewaad. Gikendamoog apii ge-nagishkodaadiwaad. Gii-makadewaabikad 'iw emikwaanens gaa-aabajitood. Agwaaweba'an zhinoodaagan anaamiindim gaa-agwindeg. Giishpin dewikweshkid, gego miinaaken omashkikiim. Nitaa-giigoonyikewag zhedeg. Nigaachidinawaa waawaashkeshi. Miskwiiwi. Iwidi inagakeyaa ani-mamiskwiiwisinoon ini aniibiishan. Gii-kwekise imaa gii-gichi-bagamaanimak gezika. Ogodaagaminaan nibi epiitaagamidenig. Owanakoninj odaabajitoon. Naadamawishin asemaawipwaagaansag, |  Awenesh dinowa. | Gaa-bikwaawiganed Indaga niisaakiiwen iwidi adaawewigamigong ji-naadamawiyan ge-agwanenjigeyaan. Ogii-naadamowaan iniw ogozisan gii-miigaanimind. Mii 'i gii-kabeshkang iwe naano-diba'igan gaa-inind ji-izhaad. Ashagi mamaajigwanebani'o wenji-naada'ogod giigoonya'. Mii dash ezhi-bazhiba'waad okoozh. Ziinzibaakwad ina, gemaa gaye doodooshaabo giwii-tagonaan gigaapiiming. Wegonen minikwewin eyaayan. Nitii na, nibi na, maagizhaa gaapii. Nindanoonig ji-ozhibii'igetamawag wii-kagwe-anokiid ji-mooshkinebii'amawag mazina'igan. Naawininj gidaa-atamawaa asemaan biindaakoonad. Atamaw ge-miijid gaazhagens. Onzaam babiiwaawan ini zhiishiibanwiinsan. Awanjish gii-niminaadagaako awe gaa-twaashing aana-gii-kina'amawind. Gidaana-onji'in ji-bakite'waasiwad a'aw animosh. Awanjish gibakite'waa. Awanjish igo niwii-kagwe-debwe. Ogii-kashkiiginaan oniijaanisensan wii'-nibe'aad. Gii-goshkozinid ogii'-aabiiginaan. Gidaa-wiidookaw ina wii-chiibaakweyaan. Giin gidaa-gabaashimaag igiw opiniig. Niizh niwii-kabaashimaag ininishibag. Bedaajiwanzwaanakik niwii'-aabaji'aa. Baamaa ningizod amik, ninga-gabaashimaa. Minomaate gijiibaakwaan. Waabooz ina gigabaashimaa. Gaawiin memwech gidaa-boozi'isii. Ninga-bima'adoo. Giishpin noondaagweweyaabikibizod gidoodaabaanish, wiiba giga-michi-bima'adoo. Gichi-gabaya'ii gii-naaniibawi naaw... naawi-aazhoganing. Ozhiigizhan waa'-inigokwegakin gimakizinikaanan. Nayaag igo nindebaabamaa biidaadagaakod. Omaa inaatenan. Odagaasaatenaan owaasakonenjigan waasa wii'-inaatenang. Bezhigwaabik geyaabi awashime nindachige. Mitikwam gidaa-agwana'aanan amikoganan. Awashishkode namadabi a'aw akiwenzii. Onzaam gizhideni besho namadabid. Ishkweyaang ninamadab odaabaaning izhaayaang oodenaang. Aaniin ezhi-wiinzod awedi ikwe nemadabid. Gego mishawaateng namadabiken. Giga-makadewaas. Ditibise 'iw makizin. Nindaana-andamawaa a'aw ikwe opiniin ji-miizhid. Bangii ningii-miinig. Gii-kiimodadaawe waabigwaniinsan wii-miinaad owiiwan. Asemaa ingii-miinigoo gii-wiikwamigooyaan. Onzaam mamaachaawan iniw makizinan gaa-pi-miinigooyaan. Daga miizhishin bezhig. Agaami-ziibi ondaagimikawe. Noopimiing ninoondawaa madwewe'od bine. Naniizaanendan epizoyan gi... gidoodaabaanens. Mookaagonasowag asiniig. Gii-pengode ninjiibaakwaan. Ningii'-waniike ji-aanji-mooshkinebadooyaan. Mii go zhigwa bapangibiisaag. Mii ganabaj igo ji-ni-gimiwang. Wawiinge gichi-bagakaatese iwe waasigan. Aandi dash gaa'-onji-noondaman i'iwe. Wiinad i'iwe adoopowinaak. Ogii-wanisidoon i'iwe mazina'igan engindangiban. Gego indawaaj andomaaken awe. Maji-mashkiki 'a eta go ogikendaan. Gego memwech ganoonaaken gimaamaa. Goshko-mawadishi. Gego babaamenimaaken gimishoomis. Megwaa apaakozige. Niwanitoonan ndaabaabika'iganan. Ningii-wanitoon niwaazakonebijigan wii-aabajitooyaan wii-waaswaayaan. Ogii-wanitoon i'iw omiskodoonechigan awe oshki-ikwe. Weweni ganawendan gidizhi'on. Giga-wanitoon igaye. Ani-baagiingwe. Naaning ningii-madaabii gii-andawaabamagwaa igiw abinoojiinyag. Niwii-madaabii noongom ishkwaa-naawakweg. Niwii-o-waambandaan injiimaan. Ingii-piigonaan iw aana-gii-minonigeyaan. Awasi-dagwaagong ningii'-ozhi'aag nindaagimag. Nashke gosha naa ezhichiged a'aw ikwezens. Nashke awedi amik biidaatiga'o. Bagidinisen. Gegaa go ani-dakate. Gegaa ingii-bichi-nisidawinawaa awe ikwe. Bakaanizi ingwana. Ambe daga da-agwaataawag igiw abinoonjiinyag. Mii go gegaa gabe-ishkwaa-naawakwe zaagagwamowaad imaa nibiikaang. Gegaa indoozhaazhishin imaa ani-zaaga'amaan. Wiisagine a'aw animosh. Nindaakoz naa. Niwaanda-wiisagine naa. Gii-noonde-bizo aana-gii-ombigwaashkwanodang Dakwaakwad 'iw okandiikan. Awegwen igo odaa-noondawaan aandi eyaanid ininishiban gaa-initaagozid. Awegwen igo gaa-mamadwetood agwajiing dibikong. Ogii-ombimaan gii-wiindamowaad iwe waa-inakamigad.., waa-inakamigadinig wii-aabita-niibinokeng. Mii miinawaa ji-gichi-inakamigak aabita-niibinokewaad. Neniizh ingii-kizhibaabatoomin iwe waakaa'igan. Ogii-piigoboonaan iniw nabagisagoon waa-aabajichigaazonipan. Ogii-mikaan 'i waazh i'imaa  endazhenid iniw boodaajibingwesiwan. Waanda-wiimbaamagad naa 'i waazh imaa nibaad makwa. Mako-bimide odapaabowen gaa-jiibaakwed. Giishpin andawendaman mako-bimide, niiyo-diba'igan gaa-akwegak bagiwaaniigin miinishin. Nindaanis ogii-kibozaanan okosimaanan. Aaniin epiitinigozid awe ayaabe gaa-paashkizwad. | Gegaa go niswaak gii-apiitinigozi. Agaami-ziibi debinaagwad manoomin. Gichi-waasa bimi-debinaagod iwe jiimaan bemi-ayaamagak. Debinaagwad 'iw Ogaakaaning iwidi agaaming. Naawi-minis debinaagwad migiziwazison. Mizhisha iwidi debinaagwad aana-gii-inag ji-o-gaadood 'iw odoodaabaan. Mii iwidi gaa-pimi-inamog ozide-miikana jiigi-ziibi. Jiigi-ziibi dananjige amik. Geyaabi jiibaakwe nimaamaa. Nising naa ninjiibaakwe noongom. Gidaa-wiidookaw ina wii-chiibaakweyaan. Giin gidaa-gabaashimaag igiw opiniig. Bekaa. Bii'aadaa awe. Nimbii'aa noozhishenh. Aweniban ji-bi-dagoshing. Akawe bii'ishin. Oodenaang niwii-izhaa Bekaa daga bii'ishin. Minopogwadoon ode'iminan. Jiigitawag gidaa-ganoonaa. Nawaj igo gagiibishe Maazhendaagod gii-noondamaang wewebinidiwaad igiweg noozis miinawaa iniw odikweman. Aaniish igo naa gaa-wii-onaapinakiiyin iwidi ataagewigamigong. | Ingii-maazhise aana-gii-o-wiikobijigeyaan. Ogii-meshkwadoonaan odoodaabaan noozis. Nimbwaanawitoon aana-wii-meshkwadoonamaan nizhoonyaa-mazina'igan. Andii ezhinizha'amawaad Zhooniyaan ningii-pi-izhinizha'amaag ningozis. Ninjaaning apii akwaakwad nindabwi. Gaawiin ganage naa nibizikitaagozisii a'awe akiwenzhiyish aana-ganoonag. Indawaaj niin indookinaa. Gii-panizi'aa bijiinaago. Gaawiin odasabiisii aana-gii-pagida'waang. Onjida nigii-panizi'igoo aana-gii-ikidoyaan wii-wiidookaazoyaan. Awenen awedi? Wiidanokiim awedi inini iwidi endananokiid. Aaniin ezhi-wiinzod awedi ikwe nemadabid. Bakaan inaajimo awedi bezhig apiich idash wa'awe. Debin awedi akik. Ogii-gichi-zegi'aan gii-apagidamowaad iniw gaa-zhiigaabiigizinid gookooko'oon. Nigichi-zegi'igonaan awe gaa-ojibinigod zhebaa. Anaamaabik ogii-izhi-gaanaan ozhooniyaaman. Anaamaabik nibaawag enigoonsag. Aaniin dasing. Mii 'i gii-pagamibizoniked awe Gakaabikaang gaa-pi-onjiid. Nizhiiwitaagana'aan 'iw wiiyaas. Ogii'-onzaami-zhiiwitaagana'aan onaboobiikaan. Ogii-kinjiba'aan iniw onaabeman aana-wii-miigaanigod. Mii awe negaji'aad iniw biindasaaganan. Jiigaya'ii iwidi ogii-padakidoon. Indaga nawadin awe abinoojiinh; onzaam jiigaya'ii imaa ayaa bagizowining. Onzaam jiigaya'ii imaa gii-niibawi gaa-onji-nawadidenig ogiboodiyegwaazon. Gaye wiin aana-gii-kagwedwe ji-ozhibii'igaazod imaa. Akawe gidaa-giigid jibwaa-gagwedweyan. Zhebaa ningii-awi-waabamaa ozhibii'igewikwe. Niwii'-wiiji'ig gaa-gii-kagwedweyaan. Aaniin minik endasoogaabawiwaad. Niishtana dasoogaabawiwag. Aapiji ingii-mashkawinig. Ganabaj gii-gotaaji. Ganabaj aanjigondaagane awe wenji-maanitaagozid. Gaawiin ganabaj odaa-gashkitoosiin ji-bawishkang manoomin. Biboonong gii-gichi-ishpaagonagaa. Biboonong gii-izhaawag nindaanis agaamakiing. Minogwaasowag igi ikwewag gashkigwaasowaad. Niizho-biboonagad gii-waabamag ishkwaaj nishiime. Gii-gichi-onzaamiino goon gii-biboonagak. Gii'-mikigaazo gaa-gii'-wanishing oshkiniigikwens. Mino-ayaa go. Ingii-waabamaag ojiindiwaad awe gizhenaabens miinawaa mindimooyenh. Noondezi awe gizhenaabens aana-giishkizhiged. Waasa ondaajimo. Aanjiwidoon iwe. Awas iwidi izhiwidoon. Gii-naabidoo'amaan i'iw zhaabonigan, ningii-kashka'oonaa a'aw asabaabiins. Gagwaadagizi 'a mindimooyenh gagwe-naabidoo'ang iwe zhaabonigan. Aaniin enaabadak o'owe zhaabonigan. / Mii owe ayaabajitoowaan gii-zhingibinagwaa amikwayaanag. Gego baapitooken ezhinaagwak. Obaapitoonan iniw omakizinishan gegwaanisago-bagoshkaanig. Ogii-paapitoon iinzan gaa-gii'-izhibii'amawag. Ona'ishimaan odoopwaaganan imaa ebinid. Otigwaanining ogii'-inaganaamaan gii-bishigwaganaandang bikwaakwad. Ganabaj ogii-kiiwashkweganaamaan. Ishpi-dibikad. Ambe gidaa-gii-kawishimomin. Aandi ezhikawed. Omaamaayan endaanid ani-izhikawe Sue.
